Li was out on business, but according to his family, Li has been living in Shanghai and managing financial businesses since leaving office and has long since given up any intention of pursuing an official career. The rumors are likely untrue. Sources have also learned that Song Zheyuan has indeed intended to have Li succeed Wang Kemin due to Wang's firm resignation, but whether Li will go north is still difficult to predict. Li is currently 57 years old and a native of Cixi, Zhejiang. He was a Jinshi in the Gui Mao year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty. He has successively served as a secretary in the Ministry of Finance, an official in the Salt Affairs Administration, a director, a financial director, a Minister of Finance, a Director-General of the Salt Affairs Administration, and a Director-General of the Currency System Bureau.

The City Chamber of Commerce Held a Design Committee Meeting Yesterday

Six Proposals Resolved

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce held the first meeting of the current Design Committee at the Chamber of Commerce at 3:00 p.m. yesterday. Twenty-one committee members attended, including Xie Xiaochu, Lu Yigeng, Zhou Bangjun, Ye Jiaxing, Pan Jiaming, Chen Weiwen, Wang Kangfang, Cai Yukun, Chu Xiaozuo, Chen Guanghai, Huang Yexin, Shen Zhongyi, Chen Jianting, Li Mulian, Gu Dongping, Gu Wensheng, Ge Weian, Yang Weisa, Hong Songjiong, and Xi Rungeng. Nine people, including Zhu Gengtao, were absent due to business. Committee member Xie Xiaochu served as chairman, with Zhu Boyuan and Wu Jichun as recorders. After the formalities were completed, the chairman reported on the proposals and began the discussion. The following resolutions were passed: 1. In the future, all companies and factories applying to the Social Affairs Bureau or the Trademark Bureau for registration, etc., must have proof from the relevant industry association or Chamber of Commerce to be valid, in order to be cautious. Resolved, passed, and submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau and the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, etc., requesting that companies and factories applying for registration in the future should be required to provide proof from the relevant industry association or Chamber of Commerce, in order to be cautious. 2. Documents that are required by government instructions to be certified by the Chamber of Commerce in order to be submitted for passport documents cannot be certified by other groups. Resolved, passed, and submitted to the Executive Yuan, requesting that all ministries and commissions issue a general order stating that documents for which local chambers of commerce are required by laws and regulations to apply for passport documents, and which must be certified by the Chamber of Commerce, should also be certified by the relevant industry association if there is to be any slight change. Other groups should not overstep their bounds. 3. Proof of goods during the anti-smuggling period should be limited to the Chamber of Commerce or the relevant industry association. Resolved, passed, and submitted to the Ministry of Finance, requesting that the Customs be ordered to ensure that proof of anti-smuggling goods during the anti-smuggling period be provided by the Chamber of Commerce or the relevant industry association, and not by other groups, in order to be cautious. 4. Industry associations with similar business natures should be merged as soon as possible. Resolved, passed, and recommended that the Chamber of Commerce establish an Investigation Committee to examine whether there are any of the above-mentioned situations in the established industry associations. If the above-mentioned situation is found, the Chamber of Commerce should submit a request to the Party and government agencies to order the merger. 5. The City Chamber of Commerce should submit the membership annual fees of members to the Review Committee for a thorough review to show fairness. Resolved, passed, and recommended that the Chamber of Commerce submit the membership annual fees of members to the Review Committee for a re-examination and charge fees in accordance with the regulations. 6. The number of executive and supervisory committee members of the City Chamber of Commerce should continue to be vigorously fought for and a request should be made to increase them, with separate regulations for special municipalities and municipal counties. Resolved, passed, and submitted to the government, requesting that the Chamber of Commerce Law be amended, and that the number of executive committee members should be separately regulated for special municipalities and municipal counties to ensure that the complexity of affairs is balanced. If approval is not granted, representatives should be sent to Beijing to argue on the basis of reason, in order to achieve thoroughness. Several temporary proposals by Committee Member Zhou Bangjun and others were submitted to the second meeting for further discussion due to lack of time.

US Expert Report: Status of Tung Tree Planting in Soviet Russia

Existing Tung Tree Forests Cover 7,500 Acres, Capable of Producing 5,000 Tons of Tung Oil After Six Years

According to the Central News Agency, Chinese vegetable oil factories are actively underway, with detailed investigations into the tung oil production of various countries for reference. Regarding the status of tung tree planting in Soviet Russia, this is based on a report by a US Department of Commerce expert. The climate in areas such as Georgia, south of the Caucasus Mountains, is mild and suitable for tung tree planting. In order to pursue development, the authorities are paying close attention to the promotion of tung forests. The Soviet government is making every effort to promote domestic tung oil production. Several years ago, a "Tung Oil Bureau" was established in Batumi on the Black Sea to actively carry out this initiative, striving to ensure that the domestic paint industry and other industries requiring tung oil do not have to rely on foreign oil supplies. Tung tree planting in Soviet Russia began 30 years ago, initially only as trial planting in the Batumi Botanical Garden. After the implementation of the first Five-Year Plan in 1930, the national paint industry rose up in demand, and the government paid attention to the tung tree planting industry. In 1934, the area of tung tree planting in Soviet Russia was only 1,000 acres. In 1935, it was expanded to 2,500 acres. Currently, tung forests cover 7,500 acres. It is expected that in two years, tung forests near Georgia will reach 25,000 acres. The current quantity of tung oil produced in Soviet Russia is still limited, but according to chemical analysis, its quality is quite good. The Soviet authorities hope that when the third Five-Year Plan is implemented, tung oil production will increase daily. It is expected that by 1942, production will increase to 5,000 tons per year, enough to meet the needs of Soviet Russia's domestic industry.

He has come to China to study the publication of fish species in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. It is reported that he is scheduled to go to Dinghai today with Chen Tongbai to use the Zhejiang Fisheries Experiment Station as a research base.

Rui Kang Collides with Yun Long

At Yuxikou, Wuhu, the Bow of the Yun Long is Broken

The Yun Long wheel of Heng'an Chengji Company in this port has a deadweight of 1,777 tons, a registration of 1,115 tons, a ship length of 228 feet, a width of 27 feet 8 inches, a depth of 21 feet 6 inches, and a draft of 19 feet. The ship is currently loading coal on the Yangtze River. The ship was scheduled to load coal at Yuxikou, across the port from Wuhu, and prepare to leave the port. However, yesterday, the captain of the ship sent an urgent telegram to Shanghai, stating that the Yun Long was suddenly collided by the Rui Kang wheel of Shou Kang Company (deadweight of 1,318 tons, length of 300 feet, width of 41 feet 7 inches, draft of 18 feet 7 inches) on the river surface at that location. The bow of the Yun Long was broken and the damage was severe. It is said that the Rui Kang only suffered minor damage. The detailed situation has not yet been reported by the shipowner. After receiving the news, the company immediately telegraphed the Yun Long shipowner to quickly report the cause of the collision and the extent of the damage, and immediately notified the insurance company to prepare for inspection of the loss and investigation of the truth about the accident.

English Tram Conductor Submits Nine Conditions to Company: Restore Work of Conductor No. 753; Dismiss Ticket Inspectors No. 25 and No. 4

According to Da Kung Pao, over 700 ticket conductors of the English Shanghai Tram Company in the Public Concession were recently dissatisfied because ticket inspectors No. 25 and No. 4 falsely reported ticket conductor Wang Jintang to the writing room on the 3rd of this month, intending to dismiss the ticket conductor. They jointly sent a letter in their names to the company manager, Evans, for relief, and proposed nine improvement conditions: (1) Restore the work of ticket conductor No. 753; (2) Dismiss ticket inspectors No. 25 and No. 4; (3) Ticket conductors and drivers must be treated equally; (4) All company employees, whether they resign or are dismissed, should be given a severance payment of one month for one year, two months for two years, and so on; (5) The inspection of military funds must be the same as the Korean ticket inspectors; (6) Chinese and Western ticket inspectors are not allowed to make unfounded reports; (7) Change the small auxiliary currency coupon price to be calculated at 28 pieces per dime; (8) Promotion from selling tickets to ticket inspectors must be based on the highest seniority and best performance, and must be tested publicly; (9) Ticket sellers and drivers must have autumn uniforms.

Prices of Miscellaneous Grains: Trending Towards Stability

Government and Merchants Emphasize Controlled Transportation and Sales

According to the Central News Agency, foreign merchants previously purchased large quantities of grain in the Yangtze River area, causing anxiety in the grain market. According to inquiries from reporters to grain merchants, foreign merchants have temporarily stopped buying in the Yangtze River area. The output of miscellaneous grains in various places this year is more abundant than in previous years. Therefore, the recent prices of miscellaneous grains are trending towards stability. However, because the late rice crop is about to be harvested, it is expected that if there are no special changes in the weather this year, the late rice harvest will be bountiful. There are concerns that cheap sales will harm farmers. Therefore, government and merchants are paying close attention to controlled transportation and sales. After the Guangdong and Guangxi incident was resolved, the supply of Siamese rice, which was originally needed annually in that area, was affected. Recently, after the Guangdong Customs imposed import duties on foreign rice, the import of foreign rice has become less cost-effective than domestic rice. Therefore, domestic rice has a lively atmosphere in Guangdong Province.

Then Shen Yuehe tried to escape and was shot and captured by the detectives. When questioned, Du Haisheng and Chen Zhihong both pushed away their confessions. Fan Gang, the agent lawyer of Lu A'gen, stood up to state his fault. Judge Tan said that the location of the incident was in the Chinese community on the road built across the border, so he ordered that the jurisdiction of the case was wrong and should be transferred to the Shanghai District Court for trial. Yang Chunshan and Chen Zhihong were ordered to be held in custody pending rescheduling because they had another case within the border.

According to the Industrial Encouragement Law, we have been approved by the Ministry of Industry for exclusive manufacturing rights, and approved by the Ministry of Finance for exemption from transit tax, and by the Ministry of Transportation and the Railway Department for reduction of transportation fees for state-run businesses. It has now been found that Yunnan Province consumes a considerable amount of calcium carbide (locally called 'coal stone'), mostly imported from foreign countries, resulting in significant losses. Because we know that your chamber has always been enthusiastic about advocating domestic goods, we hope that you will forward this to the provincial chamber of commerce, strongly promote and widely encourage the use of domestic calcium carbide, so as to maintain domestic goods and prevent losses." Upon receiving the letter, we found that the country has always used foreign goods for this calcium carbide. The company has been in operation for several years, simulating self-manufacturing, which took great effort. Now, fortunately, the products are of good quality and have been successful. All our countrymen should switch to domestic products in the future, so as not to let down the hard work of the founders and to recover economic rights. Your province is adjacent to the border with Vietnam, and preventing losses is an important task. You should be happy to promote the calcium carbide produced by the company. Therefore, we are sending this letter to earnestly request your strong support, and to promote the sale of the company's products in your region, so that domestic products can circulate smoothly and reach all places. This would be our greatest hope."

Wang Baoliang's Son from the Chaoyang Road Refugee Shantytown Requests Compassionate Allowance

Wang Baoliang, a resident of the Chaoyang Road shantytown in Pudong, died with resentment because he was forcibly evicted and beaten by the Public Works Department. His son, Chongqi, mourns his father's unnatural death and his own lack of livelihood. He submitted a petition to all the Chinese directors of the Public Works Department yesterday, saying: "Respectfully, I, the afflicted Wang Chongqi, state that my late father, Baoliang, was engaged in the business of Chinese medicine. Before January 28th, he established the Tianyi Feiyao Pharmacy at No. 53 in Chaoyang Road. His business was still able to be maintained. However, when the Shanghai Incident occurred, the losses were quite large. After the war was pacified, the market became increasingly depressed, and the business declined sharply. He had no choice but to close the business and guard his home. His life was difficult. Therefore, he moved from a flat house to a thatched cottage to avoid the wind and rain, hoping that the market would recover and he could still operate his old business. Therefore, the remaining medicinal materials and utensils were all piled in the thatched shed. Because the weather was bad, with strong winds and rain, sometimes stopping and sometimes starting, the thatched shed only existed in form and was not enough to shelter from the rain and wind. Therefore, he took the opportunity to repair it slightly on clear days to avoid the wind and rain and live in it. Unexpectedly, the Yangshupu Police Station came out to interfere and forcibly ordered its demolition. My late father repeatedly explained and reasoned with them, but was rejected. On the morning of the 2nd of this month, the police station suddenly sent a large group of seventy or eighty Chinese and Western detectives, forcibly dragging down the thatched shed at No. 448 Chaoyang Road, where the refugees lived. Passers-by were stunned, neighbors panicked, and the order was chaotic. The Chinese and Western detectives still held police batons and beat anyone they met. My late father was also beaten and injured. When the detectives withdrew, they checked the equipment, which was all crushed under the collapsed shed, in a mess that was unbearable to witness. The accumulation of several years of sweat and blood was almost completely destroyed. None of the medicinal materials and equipment were intact. My late father and mother, seeing this situation, mourned deeply and cried sadly. They even fainted. After the neighbors persuaded them euphemistically, they became mentally disturbed and lost their appetite. My late father and mother were both bedridden, and my late father passed away on the 7th of this month. My mother is seriously ill and has suffered this calamity, which has made her illness worse. She is now dying. I am also unemployed and idle. There are also my wife and two younger siblings, a family of five, who are unable to make a living. The injustice has not been redressed. I don't know when I will be able to seek redress. Rather than being in this dark situation and waiting to die, it is better to inherit the hot blood and avenge my father. Success or failure is just a death. What a pity! However, my elderly mother is old and bedridden, and I have no way to take care of her. My wife and my siblings are afraid that they will not be able to survive. Therefore, after thinking it over, I have no choice but to drink tears, endure my anger, borrow from the east and lend from the west, so as to prevent my father's bones from being exposed and to comfort his spirit. Recalling the cause of my father's death, it was actually caused by the beating by the detectives, coupled with excessive depression. In other words, it was caused by the Public Works Department. In any case, the Public Works Department cannot shirk its responsibility. Therefore, I am presenting this appeal to the Chinese directors. I implore you to show compassion, uphold justice, and seriously negotiate with the Public Works Department to ensure that the perpetrators are punished and that the survivors are given compassionate allowances, so that the living can be cared for and the dead can be comforted, justice will not be extinguished, and justice will still exist. Please also ask the Public Works Department to take into account the livelihoods of ordinary people in the future, and quickly withdraw the proposal to demolish thatched sheds, so as to benefit the people's livelihood and stabilize society. If this goal can be achieved, I will repay your kindness with utmost gratitude. I am specially making this earnest request. Please consider my plight, relieve my distress, and negotiate with the Public Works Department based on reason, giving compassionate allowances and compensation, then the gratitude will be endless."

Zhuang Jimeng and Zhang Zuming's Self-Accusation Case Was Judged Yesterday The Defendants Were All Found Not Guilty, and the Ancillary Civil Suit Was Rejected

The ancillary civil suit was rejected. Zhou Jinggeng, a compradore of the Xue Mailuo Accounting Firm at No. 9 Edward Road, ordered his employees to collect 18,000 yuan in cash from the China Industrial Bank at 3:00 PM on June 9, 1934. Not long after returning to the office, they were suddenly attacked by bandits armed with weapons, who robbed them of 12,000 yuan. After reporting to the French Concession Police Station, the suspect Zhang Zuming (shareholder of Ruichangxiang Hardware Store on Broadway Road) was arrested. According to Zhang's confession, Zhuang Jimeng (owner of Zhuangyuan Big and Small), Zhu Suyou (hardware peddler), and Tang Qingyue (president of Dade Hospital) were subsequently arrested and prosecuted by the Second Special District Court. After the trial, Zhang, Zhuang, Zhu, and Tang were acquitted. Because the Police Department appealed, the Supreme Court upheld the original judgment after three trials. After the judgment was finalized, Zhang Zuming hired a lawyer to submit a petition to the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court, accusing Zhou Jinggeng, Gao Yushu, Feng Ti, Wan Guirong, Qian Genghua, and Wang Guixiang of perjury, false accusation, and fraud, requesting an investigation, and filing an ancillary civil suit seeking 50,000 yuan in damages for reputational, emotional, and business losses. Zhuang Jimeng also believed that Zhang Zuming should not have fabricated innocent accusations, which led to his arrest and detention. He was unwilling to accept this and hired lawyer Li Guozhen to submit a petition to the First Special District Court, accusing Zhang Zuming of perjury and false accusation, and filing an ancillary civil suit seeking 50,000 yuan in damages. After the First Special District Court summoned them, it ruled that the case should be transferred to the Second Special District Court for trial because the incident occurred in the French Concession and the court lacked jurisdiction. Li Changnian, a former judge of the Second Special District Court, combined the two cases for trial and judgment. Chen Shuoying, a judge, summoned both parties to court some days ago, held a trial, announced the conclusion, and scheduled a date for the verdict. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, when the verdict was due, only Zhuang Jimeng reported to the court. Zhang Zuming, Zhou Jinggeng, and others, as well as their lawyers, did not appear. At 2:00 PM, Judge Chen arrived at the Second Criminal Court and first judged the case of Zhang Zuming's self-accusation against Zhou Jinggeng and others. The main text of the judgment was: Zhou Jinggeng, Gao Yushu, Feng Ti, Wan Guirong, Qian Genghua, and Yu Guixiang are not guilty. The fraud part is not accepted. The plaintiff's claim in the ancillary civil suit is rejected. The judgment of Zhuang Jimeng's case against Zhang Zuming stated, Zhang Zuming is not guilty. The plaintiff's claim in the ancillary civil suit is rejected.

Affected by Downstream Winds of the Yangtze River, Shanghai's Climate is Harsh Occasional Rain and Wind Patches Pacific Hurricane Stagnates

Yesterday, due to the discovery of continental monsoon winds (Depression) in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River, the atmospheric pressure in this port was quite low, with occasional rain and wind patches. The situation is recorded below:

Monsoon Develops According to the Observatory's report at 6:00 AM yesterday, after two hurricanes in the Pacific Ocean merged into one, they had advanced to within 120 nautical miles of 20 degrees north latitude and 135 degrees east longitude. The journey was very slow, showing a state of stagnation. At the same time, due to the low pressure in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River (south of Wuhu), a monsoon suddenly arose, its direction proceeding northeast.

Bad Weather This port experienced showers and rainstorms at noon yesterday, which quickly cleared up. However, after 3:00 PM, rain and wind patches reappeared, stopping only around 5:00 PM. It was also affected by the passage of the monsoon from the west in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River, so the atmospheric pressure also dropped significantly.

Automobile Driver's Union Letter to Workers on Banning Extra Gratuities

After the Shanghai Automobile Driver's Union recently received a notice from the New Life Movement Promotion Association to ban extra gratuities, the union sent comrades Zhu Weichang and Zhang Daxin to draft opinions, attend meetings, and propose discussions. The union considered that banning extra gratuities had a significant impact on the interests of all workers in the city. Therefore, it held a joint meeting of directors and supervisors at 2:00 PM on the 13th of this month to discuss it in detail and issued a letter to all workers in the city. The full text is as follows: "Our fellow automobile drivers in the city, everyone admits that the New Life Movement has been promoted throughout the country. All the bad habits and unreasonable organizations in the past, no matter how long their history, as long as they do not meet the standards of the New Life, must be abolished and reformed. The Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association recently received an order from the New Life General Association to ban the bad habit of all extra gratuities. It has convened three meetings at the Maple Bridge City Party Headquarters. All relevant groups sent responsible representatives to attend. Our union also sent Zhu Weichang and Zhang Daxin to attend the meetings, representing the hardships of the drivers in the city. After several discussions, a draft implementation plan was passed and submitted to the Shanghai New Life Movement Executive Committee for approval, and then promulgated by the city government for implementation. However, the draft has already determined the banning of extra gratuities. Our union representatives, of course, considering the hardships of the workers, could hardly agree and strongly argued at the meetings. They also stated the following four reasons: (1) Our union members work particularly long hours, day and night, and only have one day of rest after five or six days. (2) The workers' consumption during working hours is also particularly large. Every day and night, eating meals, snacks, and pocket money requires a very simple one yuan. If there are business errors, damage compensation, plus the minimum family expenses, the monthly average is at least seventy or eighty yuan. (3) Our drivers' wages are between fifteen and twenty-four yuan per month, and personal life cannot be maintained. (4) The income from gratuities ranges from forty to sixty yuan per month, and it is still received sporadically. Once banned, our main source of livelihood will be completely cut off, regardless of the lives of all the drivers in the city. The above four hardships were strongly argued at the meetings. Our union has the current responsibility to improve working conditions and protect the lives of workers. Therefore, we are informing all the drivers in the city. After receiving the notice, please come to the union within five days to offer your opinions and strive for a good way to survive. Our fellow workers in the city, do not wait and see any longer. You must understand that the New Life must be implemented, and we must also come up with proper ways to maintain our lives. Finished. Wishing you good health."

At that time, a man resembling a shop clerk was riding in a rickshaw when he was stopped by robbers posing as detectives who robbed him of a bag of legal tender. Wang Meigu, a police officer from the 21st post of the Wuzhen Road police station of the Xinzha Public Security Bureau, heard the alarm and immediately rushed to pursue the robbers. The four robbers fled east via the New Garbage Bridge in the concession. At that time, detectives Wei Sikai (transliteration), Sun Aizhong, Wang Dongchen, Qiu Zhenting, etc., from the Tilanqiao and Huisan police stations were inspecting the area. The four robbers, seeing that they were being pursued, could not stop and rushed straight into the concession. The detectives, seeing their suspicious behavior, immediately blocked their path. The robbers were about to fire their guns to resist arrest, but the detectives preemptively disarmed one robber of his box cannon and found a bag of legal tender on another robber. Knowing they were criminals, they arrested all four. At this time, the robbery victim arrived and they were all taken to the police station. An inspection of the paper bag revealed over 900 yuan of legal tender. Knowing the situation was not good, the robbers placed a handgun under the table, but it was discovered by the detectives. As the case originated in the Chinese area, they were briefly questioned before the four robbers were taken back to the scene of the crime for investigation. The robbers identified themselves as Wang Decai, 48 years old, from Yangzhou, residing in a straw shed on Qimei Road, a bamboo craftsman; Shen Xigen, 38 years old, from Donghai, residing in a straw shed in Pudong, a leather craftsman; Guo Jinfa, 33 years old, from Xuzhou, residing in a straw shed in Gaolang Bridge, a hardened robber who had previously committed robbery and served a 16-year sentence in the First Special District Court, released from prison only 17 days ago; and Yang Dashizi, 24 years old, from Yancheng, residing in a straw shed on Meizhou Road, unemployed. The box cannon was seized from Guo Jinfa, and the stolen money was found on Yang Dabaozi. The handgun also belonged to this robber. The case has now been sent to the Xinzha Branch. According to the plaintiff, Zhu Shaofang, 48 years old, from Ningbo, residing at 18 Baokang Li, Zhejiang Road, he had obtained 1,000 yuan of legal tender from the distribution office of the China Match Company in Baokang Li, Zhejiang Road, at around 10:00 AM today, and was taking it to the China Match Co., Ltd. manufacturing plant on Pingjiang Bridge, Zhonghua New Road, to pay wages. He did not expect that after passing from the concession to the Chinese area, after riding only ten steps in a rickshaw, the robbers would stop the rickshaw and rob the bag of money from behind the rickshaw. They then told him not to make a sound or they would shoot him. Questioning officer Huang Zhuojie then questioned the robbers one by one and ordered them to be taken back to the concession by the detectives, pending the dispatch of personnel to the First Special District Local Court for questioning and to request their extradition for trial.

Fuxingheng Criminal Lawsuit, Embezzlement of Silk Case, Court Orders Suspension of Trial, Civil Lawsuit in Progress

Sichuan Fuxingheng Money Shop and Tongfeng Silk Shop at 20 Jingxing Li, Tianjin Road, in this port are involved in a lawsuit in the First Special District Local Court due to a dispute over mortgaged raw silk. Li Xiangchi, deputy manager of Fuxingheng in Shanghai, initially filed a civil lawsuit against Xu Ziwu (also known as Wu Gao) and Zhu Xingzhai (also known as Shiku), managers of Tongfeng, to return the stored silk. Now, they have filed a criminal self-accusation against Xu and Zhu for embezzling the stored silk. The case has already been heard once, as reported in this newspaper. It is now known that after Xu and Zhu were sued, Zhu claimed to have left Shanghai long ago and could not be summoned. Xu hired lawyer Shen Shiyi to file a statement, stating that the defendant had never met Li Xiangchi before. The silk mentioned by the plaintiff was not a stored item, but a collateral for a loan from Li Jixiao, manager of Shanghai Qianjixiang Silk Shop, totaling over 60,000 yuan in national currency, with accounts and records to prove it. Li used the silk to obtain a loan from Tongfeng, sometimes using the name Qianjixiang and sometimes using the name Fuxingheng, without distinction. The reason for this case is that Qianjixiang owes Tongfeng over 310,000 yuan in national currency after deducting the proceeds from the sale of the mortgaged silk, and a judgment has already been issued. However, Li Jixiao, manager of the shop, harbored ill intentions, appealed the judgment to resist enforcement, and suddenly changed Qianji's business to Fuxingheng's name. Li himself secretly returned to Sichuan and colluded with Li Xiangchi, whom he had never met before, to file a civil lawsuit against Tongfeng for the return of the stored silk, intending to obtain the surplus value of the mortgage. Seeing that the civil case might result in an unfavorable judgment, he filed a criminal lawsuit as a tool of intimidation. It can be seen that the plaintiff intentionally fabricated the lawsuit. The court should find the plaintiff guilty of false accusation and suspend the trial of this case, pending the conclusion of the civil case, before proceeding. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng held a continued hearing. Defendant Xu Ziwu and his defense lawyer Shen Shiyi appeared in court and explained the previous situation, stating that although Qianjixiang and Fuxingheng have different names, they are actually the same entity. Both shops are managed by Li Jiqing, who delivered the Sichuan silk as collateral for the debt, not as stored silk as claimed by the plaintiff. Since the case is already in civil court, the court should suspend this case and wait for the civil court to resolve it. As for Zhu Xingzhai, he is old and sick and often lives in the countryside, so he could not surrender himself. Plaintiff Li Xiangchi stated that the silk was actually stored with Tongfeng for consignment sale and was later mortgaged to the Xinfu Foreign Firm on Aierduya Road. The previous civil lawsuit requested a judgment ordering the return of the stored silk, not the recovery of the silk price. Judge Huang ruled that since the case had already been filed in civil court, the court should wait for the civil court to issue a judgment, and approved the defendant's request, ordering the suspension of the trial of this case.

Ding Xiaodi Faces Additional Charge of Selling Red Pills, Many People Attended Yesterday's Hearing, Ding Claims to Be Falsely Accused by Xiao Mazi

Ding Xiaodi, a native of Changshu, has been selling rice cakes since he was a child, hence the nickname "Little Rice Cake". He is quite influential in the Xinzha area and has many apprentices. Recently, Wang Sanxiao, residing at 373, Lane 568, Xinzha Road, reported to the police that Ding led a group of people into his house on the morning of the 7th of this month and stabbed Wang five times with a knife. The police sent Wang to the hospital for treatment and attempted to arrest Ding Xiaodi. Ding heard about this and surrendered himself to the police, who sent him to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhan Liangce presided over the second criminal court hearing. The defendant hired lawyers Zhan Jifeng and Zhan Yigang to represent him. Many men and women attended the hearing. Police lawyer Jiang Baoqi rose to state the case, saying that the case was being rescheduled. The police had discovered that Ding Xiaodi was also involved in the sale of the drug "red pills", so he was now being prosecuted under Article 5 of the Provisional Regulations on the Punishment of Drug Trafficking. On July 24 of this year, the police raided two red pill trafficking locations at 69, Lane 638, Xinpu Road, and 2167, Lane 568, Xinzha Road, and arrested the perpetrators, Yao Zhongqing, etc. During the interrogation, Yao stated that the two locations were actually run by his master, Ding Xiaodi, also known as Little Rice Cake. Yao himself has been sentenced to twelve years in prison and was brought from the Western Prison to testify today. However, in recent days, the police have received several letters from residents of the Xinzha area, all of which pointed out that Little Rice Cake was usually unethical and did all kinds of bad things. Although Yao Zhongqing has been brought to the case, there are many people in the audience, all of whom are relatives and apprentices of the defendant, so he may not be willing to tell the truth. Therefore, he requested that the audience be ordered to leave. The court granted the request and ordered all the audience to leave the courtroom. Yao Zhongqing then stated that he used to work in the firewood shop opened by Ding Fuji, also known as Little Rice Cake. He was later arrested in the red pill case and sentenced to twelve years in prison. However, the red pill case has nothing to do with Little Rice Cake, and he is not an apprentice of Little Rice Cake. The mastermind behind the organization is actually Xiao Mazi Du Mou, etc. The victim, Wang Sanxiao, stated that Little Rice Cake had forced him to become his apprentice, and he refused, pointing out that he was a "little rascal". He bore a grudge and on the 6th of this month, he invited Killer Zhu A Jin, A Hao, Xiao Jiangyin, and A Jin's apprentice, etc., to beat him severely. The next morning, the defendant and five others broke into his house, held him down, and A Jin, etc., stabbed him five times. When questioned, the defendant denied all the charges, saying that Xiao Mazi Du Mou had a grudge against him and incited Wang Sanxiao to falsely accuse him. He requested a clear judgment. Judge Zhan ruled that the investigation was still ongoing and ordered the defendant to be detained pending a rescheduled hearing.

Mr. Chen Zhongting, a native of Ningdong, was a pioneer in the shipping industry. His son, Mr. Shuntong, is the general manager of the Zhongwei Shipping Company, which he founded in this port. Henan National Martial Arts Provincial Examination News

Equestrian Competition Held Simultaneously

Kaifeng Correspondence: The 6th Henan Provincial National Martial Arts Examination and Equestrian Competition will be held starting from October 5th at the Henan Stadium. Each county is limited to send three to five people, and those who apply freely are welcome. Registration starts from now until October 1st. The examination subjects are: (1) Practical: Hand-to-hand combat (boxing, wrestling), equipment competition (spear, sword, staff, sword); (2) Academic: Chinese, common sense, oral test, equestrian competition; (1) Riding: Horsemanship, bicycle; (2) Shooting: Horse archery, foot archery, slingshot. The competitors from other countries are also first-class candidates in Shanghai. The United States has decided to send personnel from the Marines to attend. The excitement of the competition at that time can be praised without saying.

You Xing Fabricates Competition Results, League Council Decides to Punish

You Xing's Score Reduced

Kang Di Promoted to Runner-Up

The Shanghai China Tennis Federation held a committee meeting yesterday to investigate Kang Di Team's evidence protesting You Xing Team's fabrication of the results of the competition with Hua Qiang Team in this year's Xian Fang Cup. After several studies, the members of the committee considered that You Xing's actions violated the spirit of sports and were inappropriate. Hua Qiang's failure to request correction and report after the incident was also negligent. It was resolved to cancel the scores of both parties in the competition to show a warning, and to instruct that everything should be based on the spirit of sports and sportsmanship in the future, and that similar events should not happen again in order to respect the spirit. According to the report, You Xing's victory over Hua Qiang was originally 15-0. Now that there is such a punishment, You Xing's current score has been reduced to 114 points (there is still the first doubles match with Xia Cun that has not been played). Kang Di will get 127 points and will be promoted to runner-up.

Education News

Guo Youshou et al. Inspect Ningxia Education

Tong Yaohua Greatly Improved After Being the Long-Term Educator

(Ningxia Correspondence) Guo Youshou, a special commissioner of the Ministry of Education, Mei Yibao, a professor at Yenching University, and Dai Leiren, a British director of the board of directors of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund and a professor of economics at Yenching University, were hired to inspect education in the Northwest. After completing the inspection in Suiyuan, they took the Eurasia jumbo jet from Baotou at 1:00 PM on September 2nd and safely arrived in Ningxia at 3:40 PM on the afternoon of the 2nd, landing at the airport outside Xiguan. Tong Yaohua, Director of the Department of Education, led important officials from the department and principals of secondary schools to welcome them. The summer training camp for primary school teachers in the province was also postponed for several days. The 300 people lined up outside Xiguan to greet the inspectors with respect in the afternoon. Guo and others entered the city and stayed at the Yinchuan Hotel. After visiting Chairman Ma in the afternoon, they were entertained by Director Tong. It was decided that at 9:00 AM on the 3rd, the welcome meeting for the entire education community of the province (all primary school teachers and persons in charge of secondary schools) would be held in the auditorium of the provincial government. Dai, Guo, and Mei gave speeches respectively, giving encouragement. The meeting ended at 11:00 AM. In the afternoon, Guo and others inspected Ningxia Middle School, Ningxia Normal School, and Hui People's Normal School. At the request of Chairman Ma, a banquet was held at Lumu Tower. On the 4th, accompanied by Director Tong and Chief Secretary Yang, they went to Dingyuanying (240 miles from the provincial capital) and arrived in the afternoon. Local primary school students lined up to welcome them, and Dafu hung the Party and National flags to pay their respects. They stayed at the Dafu Guesthouse. They then visited Prince Dali Zhaya to inquire about the education of the Mongolian banner. On the morning of the 5th, after inspecting Dingyuanying Primary School in Alashan Banner, they went to Nan Temple (Lama Temple), which was 60 miles away, to visit. In the evening, they attended Dafu's banquet at Dafu. Dafu paid close attention to the improvement of the living conditions of the Mongolian people. He specially sent a letter to the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund, requesting subsidies for the improvement of animal husbandry and public health, and prepared a letter to Chairman Zhu Liuxian, which was forwarded by Director Dai, which was sufficient to show Dafu's enthusiasm for governing the banner. On the morning of the 6th, they departed from Dingyuanying and arrived in Ningxia at 1:00 PM. At 3:00 PM, accompanied by Director Tong, Inspector Pi, and primary school instructors, they went to various counties to inspect. First, they went to Ningsuo (60 miles from the provincial capital) and inspected various schools, and then stayed at the county government. On the morning of the 7th, they set off again, passing through Xiaoba to see the Han Yan Canal irrigation, and decided to go to Daba to see the Tang Lai Canal irrigation. At noon, they arrived at Zaowei Fort in Zhongning County to inspect the Zaoyuan County Primary School. At about 4:00 PM in the afternoon, they arrived at Zhongwei County (360 miles from the province) and stayed at the Provincial Zhongwei Middle School, and inspected the school conveniently. On the morning of the 8th, they inspected the county primary school, which had more than 300 students and was the largest primary school in the province, the girls' primary school, and the short-term primary school. They set off at noon and arrived in Ningxia at 8:00 PM in the evening. On the morning of the 9th, they visited the Ningxia Health Experiment Office and inspected the Provincial Senior Midwifery School, Girls' Middle School, Experimental Primary School, and Literacy Class. Finally, they said goodbye to Chairman Ma and took a plane to Lanzhou in the afternoon. Before leaving, the fat reporter inquired about Guo's impression of this inspection of education and replied that since Tong Yaohua, Director of the Department of Education, has been in charge of education in Ningxia Province in the 24th year, both the quality and quantity have improved. The large-scale summer training camp held this year includes all primary school teachers, local education administrators, and secondary school students, which is indeed a new initiative in Ningxia's education and is of great benefit to the promotion of education. As for the education of the Mongolian banner in Ningxia, Alashan Banner has established five primary schools, and is preparing to establish a girls' primary school, with Dafu's wife as the principal, which is sufficient to show Dafu's enthusiasm for education. Finally, he praised the scenery along the Yellow River and the convenience of the canals, which are deeply sufficient for the development of the Chinese people. Ningxia Province has a very promising future.

Recent News on the Compilation and Translation of Terminology by the National Institute for Compilation and Translation

Recent news on the compilation and translation of terminology by the National Institute for Compilation and Translation is summarized below: (1) The second review of the terminology of chemical instruments and equipment has been sent to various experts and the annual meeting of the Chinese Chemical Society for review and discussion. The society has resolved that the institute will organize and print the compound name part of all the terms according to the initial review opinions as the second review of the second volume, and send it to various experts for joint review with the first volume, so that all corrections can be made. This part of the compound name is currently being organized and will be printed and sent for review within the next month. The institute will submit a request to the Ministry of Education at the end of the year to convene a meeting of the Instrument Terminology Review Committee to make a final decision. (2) The ordinary part of the electrical engineering terminology was originally scheduled to convene various review committee members in Beijing in September for a review meeting to make a decision. It was planned to start transcribing and printing the opinions of all parties into volumes from August 17 for application during the meeting. Now, because there are too many words and the opinions of all parties are divided, the transcription and printing work is time-consuming and it can be printed on schedule. After consulting with Chairman Yun, it was agreed to change the meeting to start on October 4. As for the meeting expenses, the Ministry of Education has approved a subsidy of 500 yuan. (3) The mechanical terminology has been organized and completed by Professor Yang Jia Yu and Chen Daxie of Central University. After the alphabetical order is sorted out, it will be transcribed into volumes and submitted for review. (4) The botanical terminology has been sent by the institute to various members for review, and Luo Zonglu, Yu Dahuan, and Li Shunqing have reviewed and returned a copy. Another part has also been compiled by Wang Zengjia and edited by the institute, totaling 3,263 entries. It is now being transcribed and will be distributed to various members for review again.

Wu Baojin Returns Home After Studying in Japan

Impressions of His Time in Japan

Wu Baojin, former secretary of the Municipal Security Bureau, was dispatched last year to study in Japan and Germany. He first went to Japan and was admitted to the graduate school of Tokyo Imperial University. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday aboard the President McKinley and is staying at the New Asia Hotel. Our reporter made a special trip to interview him, and his remarks are as follows:

There are many reasons for Japan's current state. To summarize the main points, the country's small size makes it easy to develop and govern. Moreover, the country is surrounded by the sea, which makes transportation convenient and facilitates contact with other countries' cultures. Therefore, it has been able to absorb the strengths of Western Europe while discarding its own dross. In addition, after the Meiji Restoration, the feudal lords returned power to the emperor, thus unifying the country in both name and reality and stabilizing social order. This was also aided by the establishment of a police system and the beautiful customs of diligence, frugality, and imitation among the people, as well as the division of labor between husbands and wives. Almost everyone in the country, directly or indirectly, participates in public and private production. They have few extravagant or wasteful habits and few bad habits, so social problems are less common than in other countries. In recent years, the country's foreign trade has had a monthly surplus. At a time when the entire global economy is in recession, its goods are still able to compete in various markets. This is undoubtedly due to its low prices, high quality, and unique management methods. Furthermore, the government allows people, especially intellectuals, to continuously improve their treatment and provides them with equal opportunities in their careers. This not only allows them to fully utilize their talents but also reduces the number of unemployed. Therefore, the general livelihood—the so-called "basic standard of living"—is relatively stable.

In the country, most low-level occupations and light industries are occupied by women. This not only cultivates women's sense of serving the country and sharing its burdens and gaining economic independence but also forces men to engage in heavy industry and aspire to great achievements.

The cultural level of the country is high. Since the implementation of a six-year compulsory education system (the Ministry of Education recently proposed extending it by two years), illiteracy has almost disappeared. Moreover, the proliferation of supplementary, technical, and vocational education, as well as the abundance of books and magazines, and the rapid introduction and dissemination of new knowledge from other countries, can be said to be a culmination of translations from various countries.

Japan and Russia can be called the hegemons of the Far East. After the Russo-Japanese War, Japan jumped into the ranks of the great powers. In addition, its coastal location and lack of domestic raw materials have prevented it from being coveted by developed countries. Therefore, in order to survive and defend its nation, it has instead gained the opportunity to rapidly expand its army, navy, and air force and expand its foreign markets. It has a strong sense of being the sole leader in Asia. Triggered by the Manchurian Incident, due to its geographical proximity, economic, political, and military conflicts with Soviet Russia often arise, and there have even been intentional or impulsive steps towards conflict. Domestic public opinion has been boiling as a result. However, this is merely empty rhetoric in written battles. In reality, concrete actions by both sides are not imminent.

On the other hand, due to the country's natural advantages and the diligence and fortitude of its people, it has been able to join the ranks of modern emerging nations. However, because its national strength relies heavily on external forces for its self-sufficiency in production, it has the regret of being hollow and upside-down at its core. Moreover, the annual budget is inflated, and the people feel burdened by taxes and public debt. This is a point that cannot but be worried about. As for the inside and outside of its society, it cannot exceed the scope of the iron rules of the current system. However, general observers are prone to superficiality, only observing its one-sided advantages and forgetting deeper observation. Yet, deeper understanding requires a longer period of time to delve into the depths of society and experience it in many ways. Looking back at our country's long history and unique culture, and based on the research of scholars from various countries, the Chinese people's excellent minds, broad minds, sharp thinking, and far-sighted vision are all top-notch. Therefore, the following is expected:

Select outstanding young adults from across the country for organized military spirit, vocational skills, and practical training in international knowledge, preparing them to be powerful new cells for national rejuvenation, so that they can one day fill the ranks of various production departments and the pillars of national defense.

Indeed, there are more things that China should develop than any other country at present, so the need and cultivation of talent are also more urgent than in other countries. We can take advantage of the frequent external turmoil and the subtle international relations to create an opportunity for the revival of national fortune. The whole country should conduct a census of talent so that they can be assigned to various tasks, ensuring that knowledge is applied and efficiency is increased in various undertakings. Without violating the law or affecting public order, they should be granted freedom of thought, so that the spirit of all countries can be extended and a wide range of unique insights and objective comments can be offered to the country. Instead of regarding them as a social hindrance, it is better to gather and channel them to transform them into a cohesive force for the masses.

After carefully selecting and employing those who have clarified history and governance, it seems appropriate to implement a lifetime employment system, a pension system, reduce administrative regions, cut superfluous agencies, clarify rewards and punishments, eliminate bad habits in the bureaucracy, purify personnel in the officialdom, raise the salaries of middle and lower-level employees, and consolidate their duties. In this way, both the method of governance and the people being governed will be well-prepared, which may be beneficial to the future of the country.

The situations of different countries are different, so their needs are different. It seems inappropriate to blindly adopt or imitate other countries while obliterating a country's uniqueness and creativity.

Overseas Chinese deeply appreciate the motherland's years of continuous progress and policy measures, as they are keenly aware of the stimulation of external pressure and hope for the motherland's revitalization. They deeply hope that the people of the country will not betray their ardent expectations. This trip was hasty, so I am only publishing one aspect of my observations. If there is an opportunity in the future, I will discuss it in a special article.

Radio Station: People's Education Hall

Zhou Houxu, Candidate for the National Assembly Education Association, on His Opinions on Today's Education

Twenty Opinions Expressed

Zhou Houxu is participating in this year's National Assembly Education Association election. Mr. Zhou is from Jiangdu, Jiangsu, and holds a master's degree from the Massachusetts Institute of Technology in the United States. He has traveled to Europe, America, and Japan to observe education. He has served as a professor at the former National Guangdong University, Southeast University, and Henan Zhongzhou University. He is currently the principal of Yangzhou Middle School in Jiangsu Province, a position he has held for ten years. The school's status and management achievements have long been known to the public and need not be elaborated. His writings have been published in various newspapers and magazines. Our reporter met with him yesterday. Mr. Zhou expressed his support for open and fair elections, which are followed by various countries around the world, and also the demeanor that educators should have, and he is happy to be the first to advocate for it and create a fair election atmosphere. The reporter then asked him for his views on future education. Mr. Zhou summarized his usual performances and recent claims and presented them to each point for publication:

(1) The highest principle of education in our country should be to reward integrity and revive the nation, and the necessary path should be to concentrate national strength to engage in production and national defense construction. (2) Strive to promote the popularization of compulsory education, shorten the completion period, and strictly formulate supervision and assessment methods. (3) Elementary education should focus on the physical development of children and the development of good habits, and should not focus on the instillation of knowledge. (4) Educational funding should be expanded year by year. New taxes, such as income tax, inheritance tax, and land appreciation tax, should be allocated to educational funding to develop compulsory education and improve the treatment of elementary school teachers. (5) Youth training should focus on spiritual training and physical training. (6) Youth spiritual training should establish guidelines, such as cultivating integrity, sacrificing oneself for the group, being loyal to the nation, observing discipline, and obeying leaders, and establish detailed implementation methods for schools at all levels. (7) Youth physical training should focus on military operations and outdoor living, and should focus on universal development to be able to endure hardship and adapt to the extraordinary needs of the country. (8) In addition to general knowledge and civic training, ordinary women's education should focus on physical training, household operations, and vocational training. (9) Vocational education should be implemented separately in each vocational area. The number of students should meet the needs of each locality. It is not necessary to rigidly establish a standard of funding proportion with middle schools and normal schools, and make unreasonable expansions. Living education that suits the needs of the nation should be promoted as much as possible throughout the country. (10) Scientific education in primary and secondary schools should strive for popularization and practical application. Equipment should be enriched, experiments should be emphasized, and in universities, research should be emphasized with the goal of production and national defense. In social education, it should strive to be popular. (11) Talent education should select young people with special talents and provide them with special education to develop their strengths. (12) The association and old system should be improved to adopt a stratified and categorized random examination method, so as not to hinder the physical and mental development of young people. (13) Entrance examinations for schools at all levels and various examinations, in addition to focusing on knowledge testing, should also test the study of physical education, labor, and art to promote it. (14) When the ratio of the number of candidates to the number of admissions is too large in entrance examinations for schools at all levels, overall planning should be made to seek relief to reduce the pain and danger of out-of-school youth. (15) Establish and implement the system of seniority pay for primary and secondary school teachers, and the method of resting for one year after serving for nine years, and make a clear order to protect the position of teachers, so that they can serve with peace of mind and regard education as a lifelong profession. (16) Primary and secondary school teachers have great responsibilities and lead hard lives, so a reward system should be established to show respect and encouragement. Children of teachers should be given special treatment in school admission. (17) Teacher training aims to train outstanding young people. In addition to knowledge study, it should also focus on character cultivation and physical training. (18) Teacher training should be encouraged in many ways and given ample opportunities. (19) Encourage excellent private schools and private schools to make up for the shortcomings of public schools. (20) Social education should strive to penetrate into the people and emphasize the training of production, national defense, and national consciousness.

Finance: Gold Swap Day Benchmark Falls Slightly by Seven Cents, Big Holders Cover Shorts...Longs Also Sell

Yesterday, the gold market fell by another seven cents due to the continued decline in pure gold and the slight increase in the swap premium. In the morning, it was said that the overseas silver market was calm in both England and America, and that after the close, India sold a small amount, but the US Treasury Department bought it, and the market stabilized. Forward silver prices in Monterrey were unchanged, exchange rates rose, London raw gold fell by one penny, and the Central Bank's exchange rate announcement showed both England and America unchanged. The customs gold unit fell by two percent, and the benchmark gold price was announced to be 1,117.5 yuan. The pre-market trading was weak due to sales from Shengyuan Yong and Yuanmaoyong. The morning opened lower, and continued to decline due to sales from large holders after the opening. Buyers took advantage of the low prices to maintain, and it was easy to rebound. The HSBC exchange rate announcement showed both England and America unchanged, and the silver equalization tax remained unchanged. At this time, it was extremely calm and only fluctuated. Later, as the supply decreased slightly, buying became more active, and the trend stabilized at noon. In the afternoon, the market became slightly weak again due to the swap premium rising. However, after the opening, the overall situation was peaceful, with only a three-cent fluctuation. The swap was posted by the longs at 2.78 yuan yesterday. The market situation for today is recorded below.

The morning opened at 1,121.7 yuan, down seven cents from the previous close. Yuanmaoyong unloaded and retreated to 1.4 yuan. Dadecheng, Qiafengyong, Yuanmaoyong paid the fee, rising to 1.8 yuan. Chunyuan Yong had some supply. The HSBC exchange rate announcement showed both England and America unchanged, retreating to 1.6 yuan. The silver equalization tax announcement showed no change, and there was also no change. Later, Fuxingyong, Qiafengyong, and Jinfengyong all bought, and the noon closed rose to 1,122.1 yuan.

The afternoon opened at 1,121.7 yuan, Dingkang sold to 1.6 yuan, and Chunyuan Yong paid the fee, rising to 1.9 yuan. Dingkang and Dachangxiang unloaded, and it fell slightly. Finally, there was a lack of trading, and the close was 1,121.7 yuan.

The closing price, based on the Central Bank's standard benchmark gold price announcement, fell to 1,117.5 yuan, which was about 4 yuan higher than the closing price. The current month's book value was 1,119 yuan, and October's book value was 1,122 yuan. The morning's water replenishment was 1,119 yuan. Red gold was priced at 8 yuan more, at 1,129.7 yuan. The spot market was mediocre. Tianjin goods were priced at 13.5 yuan more, and cooked red gold was priced at 11.5 yuan more, but there were no sellers. Sellers were priced at 15 yuan more, but there was no red gold traded. There were still 672 remaining slips for this month, with 9 long parties and 5 short parties.

Trading in the market was normal. In summary, Chunyuan Yong (Fuda was allocated 256 slips at 21.6 yuan), Qiafengyong (Yicheng was allocated 567 slips at 22 yuan), Qingfayong, Futaiyong, Lifeng, Dadecheng, etc. were on the buying side, while Dingkang, Qianchangxiang, Yuanmaoyong, Shengyuan Yong, Tongfeng, Hengyu, Xixiang, Huixiang, Yongde, Dachangxiang, and Tongfu, etc. were on the selling side. Hengyu advanced and then exited, while Yuanmaoyong and Chunyuan Yong exited and then advanced.

The market situation for the day was weak. The morning opened at 1,121.7 yuan, and the close was 1,121.7 yuan. The highest price was 1,122.1 yuan, and the lowest price was 1,121.4 yuan, with a fluctuation of seven cents. As a result, it fell by seven cents compared to the previous close.

The initial price for this year's October/November swap was posted by the longs at 2.34 yuan. Although Dadecheng had a premium, Longs Hengyu, Wanxing, Shenkang, Fuxingyong, Fuyu, Qiafengyong, and Wuchangxiang all posted premiums, gradually rising to 2.78 yuan. Dadecheng, Yuanmaoyong, Qianchangxiang, and Jingfu Yicheng took advantage of the high price to post premiums, falling to 2.5 yuan. Fuyu, Hengyu, Huixiang, Hengchang, Yongfuxing, Yong still came to post premiums. At 2:30 PM, when the official opening began, the sellers posted a premium of 2.8 yuan, and Tongfeng, Hengchunyuan Yong, and Yiyu posted premiums. Yuanmaoyong, Dachangxiang, etc. posted premiums, and the price hovered between 2.7 and 8 yuan. The closing price was 2.7 yuan. The total number of transactions for the day was 1,792 slips in the morning and 8,407 slips in the afternoon.

Among the October slips that have not yet been swapped, Longs include Dachangxiang 700+, Qiafengyong 300+, Fuxingyong and Dadecheng 110+ each, and shorts include Chengdai 300+, Huixiang and Dafeng, Heng Chunyuan Yong 200+ each, and Runchangyu and Daheng 100+ each. The total remaining number is 1,715 slips, with 12 long parties and 15 short parties.

The November lineup includes Longs Qiafengyong 1,000+, Hengchangyong, Wanxing, and Fuxingyong 700+ each, Huixiang 500+, Wuchangxiang 400+, Shenkang and Dachangxiang 300+ each, Yuanmaoyong and Qingfayong 200+ each, Shunli, Fuyu, and Dingkang 100+ each, and shorts include Tongfengheng 1,300+, Dadecheng 1,000+, Shengyuan Yong 500+, Chunyuan Yong and Yuanchangyong 300+ each, and Jingfu, Jiuda, Chengda, Qianchangxiang, Runchangyu, Yiyu, Futaiheng, Tongtaichang, Yida, Dafengheng, Shenyong, and Tongfu 100+ each. Exchange Rates Rise, Banks Tighten, US Dollar Becomes Easier Again

Yesterday, the foreign exchange market saw exchange rates rise and the US dollar become easier again, and banks tightened. In the morning, it was reported from overseas that the London large slips were calm in both near and far months, and that after the close, India sold slightly, but it was bought by the US Treasury Department, and the price was still flat. The Free Sale of Chinese Tea in New South Wales and the Effectiveness of Tea Inspection

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry has always been very strict with the inspection of export commodities, hoping that the quality of export commodities will become increasingly refined, and overseas markets will gradually be opened up. The inspection of export tea is even more emphasized. Those who pass the inspection are given a certificate of conformity before being allowed to export. Therefore, the quality of Chinese tea is steadily improving. According to a report from the Consulate in Wellington, tea exported to New South Wales has always been inspected by the local health bureau. Only those that are deemed qualified are allowed to be sold, and those that are unqualified are not allowed to be sold, and a fine of one pound and one shilling must be paid for the inspection fee. Although most of the Chinese tea exported to New South Wales in the past was allowed to be sold, it was limited to being sold to Chinese people for drinking. Because the Chinese merchants had to submit the tea for inspection, which was time-consuming, and because it was often deemed unqualified, they had to pay the inspection fee. Therefore, most of them directly recognized that the tea quality was unqualified and sold it exclusively to Chinese people. This method has been in place for a long time, causing great losses to China's foreign trade in tea, and causing the reputation of Chinese tea to be tarnished. At this time when China is promoting international trade, it is extremely difficult to allow this practice to continue. The Chinese Consulate in Wellington believes that since Chinese tea has been inspected and qualified by government agencies before being allowed to be exported, there is no need to conduct another inspection on the tea that comes to New South Wales. After negotiations with the New South Wales government, it was requested that imported Chinese tea be exempted from inspection and allowed to be sold freely without special restrictions. The New South Wales government has replied by letter, stating that in the future, Chinese tea that is imported and has been inspected and qualified by the Chinese government with a certificate can be exempted from inspection and will no longer be restricted to being sold to Chinese people.

Cotton Yarn: The Yarn Market Still Faces Heavy Pressure

The yarn market experienced a morning drop followed by a recovery in the afternoon, with momentum returning to a state of fluctuation. However, speculators and large traders generally leaned towards selling, exerting significant pressure. Nevertheless, current yarn customers have robust demand, so selling prices remain firm, and the inventory in warehouses is gradually decreasing.

This Month Alone Drops 1.3 Yuan

At the opening of the forward yarn market, due to unfavorable overseas yarn and cotton market conditions, prices for all months showed a consistent downward trend. Trading in the market was loose and sluggish, with most people expecting declines. Prices for each month fell by six, seven, or eight cents. Second round trading varied, fluctuating by two or three cents. Third round traders offered support, leading to a sudden drop of seven or eight cents. By the close of trading, short sellers continued to exert pressure, and market conditions changed rapidly. Near-term months fell by seven cents to 1.2 yuan, while far-term months fell by seven or eight cents. Checks revealed that Gengfeng, Runkang, and Fukang were buying heavily, but this still could not curb the speculative atmosphere. Yuda, Taichang, and Hengchang, on the other hand, significantly increased their short positions. The forward yarn trading resulted in price declines for all months compared to the previous day's closing price, ranging from six, seven, eight, or nine cents to 1.4 yuan. The market situation rose slightly at the afternoon opening due to large traders pushing in, leading to a step-by-step increase in the market as inventory was relatively tight. However, a certain individual continued to exert pressure on this month's contracts, further weakening them. Far-term months were relatively firm. As a result, prices for all months rose compared to the morning closing price, by one, two, four, five, or six cents. Checks revealed that Dafu sold 2,100 bales, Yuda 1,050 bales, Huamao 650 bales, Shenji 1,250 bales, Taichang 2,200 bales, Yichang 650 bales, Xiacheng 1,450 bales, Hengchang 1,150 bales, and Chengji 1,100 bales. Jinchang bought 1,050 bales, Juxing 1,150 bales, Gengfeng 2,600 bales, Senkang 800 bales, Runkang 2,000 bales, and Xincheng 700 bales. Active Spot Demand, Forward Cotton Falls and Then Recovers

The cotton market initially fell in the morning due to a pullback in U.S. cotton and weakness in Indian cotton. Widespread short selling led to declines. Subsequently, Changhe and Runkang covered their short positions, while long positions were increased. Both sides competed fiercely, market momentum was mixed, and the spot cotton market was favorable. In the afternoon, the market recovered.

Cotton: No Fluctuations

The cotton forward market opened with U.S. cotton weakening and falling by 8 to 14 points, Indian cotton falling by 1 or 2 rupees, and Osaka Sanpin cotton falling by 3 or 4 cents. Market sentiment was weak, and selling pressure was strong. Prices for all months fell by 1.5 to 2 cents. During the second trading session, due to the efforts of Gengfeng, Changhe, Runkang, and Ruida to push prices up, both long and short positions emerged, recovering 5 to 15 cents. By the third trading session, news of weakness in the yarn market caused retail and large traders to exert pressure on October contracts, and the market retreated again. Dafu, Chengji, Yuda, Renfeng, Wang Taixing, Taichang, Changfeng, Shengyuan, and Yongda sold heavily. The forward cotton trading resulted in price declines for all months compared to the previous day's closing price, ranging from 2 to 3.5 cents. At the afternoon opening, previous short positions were covered, and large quantities were bought. In addition, active demand for spot cotton boosted sentiment, and prices jumped by 2 or 3 cents. The market retreated slightly at the close of trading. As a result, prices for all months rose by 2.5 to 4 cents compared to the morning closing price. Summary of Yarn and Cotton Exchange News

Refund of Special Margin: The Shanghai Yarn and Cloth Exchange has been collecting a special cash margin of 8 yuan per bale for new cotton yarn transactions and 3 yuan per dan for new cotton transactions since September 3, as well as collecting margin from one party for new two-way accounts. It is now announced that these measures will be canceled from the 15th onwards. The previously collected margin will be refunded starting today (the 16th).

Holiday and Settlement Date: The settlement date for September standard yarn and cotton is set for the 28th of this month. Trading of September standard yarn and cotton will be suspended on the 24th, 25th, and 26th. The market will also be closed on the settlement date. Additionally, September 30th, the traditional Mid-Autumn Festival, will be a temporary market holiday.

Overseas Cotton and Yarn Prices Both Decline

Yesterday, the US cotton market opened with unsteady conditions, as prices for all months varied from a drop of three points to a rise of two points. Early in the morning, sales were made by Southern and local entities. Subsequently, purchases were made by peers and Liverpool for October and by Wall Street for December. Market prices recovered, but then due to sales from the South, the number of settlements increased drastically, causing a large drop in market price. Some people are paying attention to October contracts, and some are making both near and far-term hedges due to rumors that inventory could increase. The market closed flat and weak. Spot prices fell by 10 points, and futures prices fell by 6 to 14 points. English cotton spot prices fell by one point, and futures prices fell by 5 or 6 points. Indian cotton initially rose due to purchases by speculators and operators, but weakened later due to sales from European exporters and profit-taking. Piece Goods: Autumn Sales Special, Spot Cotton Cloth Demand Exceeds Supply

Yesterday's cotton cloth market, due to the opening of sales in various regions, although Dongpi white goods were affected by the decline in yarn and cotton prices, falling by 2.5 cents per piece, Qingdao's 14-pound Double Dragon Pearl fine cloth was the strongest in the market due to its scarcity in Shanghai. Currently, various factories are rushing to weave grey cloth, resulting in a significant shortage of finished products. For example, fine cloth and fine twill from factories such as Shanghai Dakang and Tongyu require waiting one to two weeks for a complete empty warehouse order before delivery. The supply of white goods from local factories remains significantly insufficient. Shenxin Factory, which originally produced the most, is now only producing 10 to 20 percent. The price of Xinyu Factory's Earth fine cloth rose by 1 cent per piece, and the price of 18-pound Racing coarse cloth rose by 5 cents due to a lack of goods arriving from Hankou. Coarse cloth and fine twill from various factories are all very attractive. The prices of Chinese and foreign colored cloths are particularly firm and popular, and manufacturers are experiencing a shortage of goods to meet demand. This is because there have been abundant harvests in various regions this year, and the demand for cotton cloth is very strong. Therefore, even if cotton prices fall in the future, the cotton cloth market may still be able to maintain its current momentum.

National Goods Female Interviewers

— Ignorant

This time the city's national goods movement federation, in order to awaken a group of numb and obsessed women who love to buy foreign goods, specially recruited female interviewers, is in formal training, will soon begin to work. Although only three, but the author hopes that they can complete the immense mission they bear!

Indeed, in Shanghai alone, the import of foreign goods, in addition to machinery, clothing, food and cosmetics, accounts for the majority, from shark fins and rouge, in recent years, the shocking number of imports, can get a considerable proof. But these things, are not all through the hands of the housewife? If the housewife is determined not to use foreign goods, then shark fins and rouge, etc., how can they invade the family?

It can be seen that female interviewers go to each dispatched family to interview housewives, expounding the danger of loving foreign goods, which can promote the destruction of China, and turn around to use national goods, which is certainly an important work, directly promoting national goods, and indirectly saving the country. There is more than one way to promote national goods, female interviewers are just one kind of thing that people engaged in the national goods movement have thought of. In the past, all comrades who participated in the national goods movement, oral speeches, written works, and the organization of national goods exhibitions, etc., were also important work, were they not?

But unfortunately, those noble women, modern ladies, someone gives a speech on national goods issues, do not go to listen, newspapers and magazines, rarely look at once or twice a year, as for the national goods exhibition, national goods market, national goods movement, etc., then they have long made up their minds, not to buy some things. Therefore, you despite trying all kinds of methods to promote the national goods movement, they still buy foreign goods as much as possible, what does not matter.

Okay, now by female interviewers to each family, or in women's groups to visit, then just receive, those noble housewives, modern ladies, female interviewers' advice and election, in any case, should be audible, compared to the national goods exhibition, the national goods movement and them, naturally can be more close and effective.

However, female interviewers visit each family, whether the housewife entertains, after the reception, whether to accept the advice? There are still many problems, of course, there are still many difficulties. In Shanghai's situation, if you can not say important things to meet with the owner, immediately rejected by the servants or the guards, is also a common thing. That is, open you in, see the housewife, because you are not related to the people, when you an uninvited guest, look at her white eyes, subject to her cold treatment, is not rare. Therefore, when a female interviewer conducts interview work, she must at least have a spirit of perseverance and full of patience, not afraid of difficulties, not afraid of suffering, endure ridicule, and look at people's cold faces, in order to use various methods to advise housewives to turn around and not use foreign goods.

On the other hand, we deeply know that Shanghai is a very wide place, only three female interviewers, in a short period of time, how can we go through all the families? Therefore, after the female visit begins to work, if effective, we deeply hope that the national goods movement federation can add a few more; At the same time, in major cities outside of Shanghai, groups that promote the national goods movement should also legally employ female interviewers.

— Meng Zhao

Good news came, the national goods female interviewers, will begin to implement interview work! This is a new record in the citizens' national goods year!
