Counseling by Example

— Rong Yu

I have read many articles in newspapers and magazines saying, "Students should use the summer vacation to persuade the public to buy domestic goods." At first glance, I thought this was a good idea, because students are intellectuals, and people have a certain respect for them; moreover, they have sharp minds and persuasive eloquence, and their publicity is bound to achieve twice the result with half the effort. However, upon careful study, it is just on paper and absolutely impossible. The reason is very simple, because most students today are promoters of foreign goods. They wear foreign clothes and use foreign goods. How can you ask them to promote the use of domestic goods? Wouldn't that be a great joke? Perhaps students will get angry when they read this, but this is the truth, without any slander. Therefore, I say that instead of asking students to persuade others during the summer vacation, it would be a practical way for them to make a determination to use domestic goods first.

Students have a sharp pen to write a few articles on using domestic goods, and a silver tongue to talk about saving the country, but the reality is just the opposite. I think this is a shameful thing. A few years ago, I followed a domestic goods propaganda team to work in the countryside. In a teahouse, we met an old gentleman with a rigid mind. He listened to the speeches of several team members, and at first he nodded and applauded, expressing his approval. Later, the old gentleman suddenly noticed that one of the team members was wearing a Western suit under his gown. He suddenly slammed the table and shouted, calling him "a beast in clothing!" and "outwardly benevolent and righteous, but inwardly a male thief and female prostitute!" He roared like a madman. Despite repeated explanations, he would not stop. Some busybodies also echoed him. As a result, not only was the publicity unsuccessful, but we had to retreat in defeat. The lesson learned from this incident is that to persuade others, you must first "lead by example."

Hua Yi Industrial Cooperative's Security Lamp

Recently, many Chinese people have made new inventions in industrial products and have applied to the government for patents, which shows the rapid progress of domestic production. Among them is a chemical battery security lamp invented by Zhu Jianlin and Liu Ziyi. It is made entirely of domestic goods. It relies on chemical action to generate electricity. Its light is no different from ordinary electric lights, and it is half as economical as kerosene. Moreover, it is convenient to use and has no danger. The Ministry of Industry has approved the patent, and the manufacturing plant is located at 963 Dongjing Road, Shanghai. The scale is grand, the equipment is precise, and it is managed entirely by scientific methods. It is divided into five groups: machinery, manufacturing, medicine preparation, materials, and electricity. They are working actively. It is expected that this lamp will be welcomed by the society when it is launched. From then on, the light will spread far and wide. Even in remote areas without electric lighting equipment, people can enjoy the benefits of electric lights. This is truly a good phenomenon in the domestic goods industry.

Author's Important Correction

In my previous article in this journal, "The New Activity of the Domestic Chemical Electric Essence Lamp," I mentioned that Hua Yi Industrial Cooperative had temporarily stopped operations. Now, after investigation, this is absolutely not true. According to the Ministry of Industry, Hua Yi Industrial Cooperative's patent has been clarified and received long ago, and its business scope extends to various regions, with outstanding reputation. I am afraid that the outside world will spread false information by mistake, so I specially make this solemn correction to clarify the facts and express my sincere apologies! Autumn Man respectfully.

Contribution

Factory Visits and Home Visits

— Yang An

Five ladies are responsible for home visits, shouldering a great mission. They will depart to the western part of Shanghai soon to conduct home visits. Before their departure, they first make factory visits, which is of great significance and the steps are very proper. It is imperative to elaborate on this:

The purpose of visiting housewives is to explain the importance of promoting domestic goods. However, promoting domestic goods cannot be done with empty words. There must be genuine knowledge and insight to tell people the actual situation and objects. All raw materials collection, manufacturing procedures, new working conditions, and their effects and advantages should be explained one by one, as clear as a palm. Then they can gain the housewife's confidence and arouse their enthusiasm for using domestic goods. In particular, how to use, store, maintain, and be economical in using a certain product should be delivered in a guiding manner, tireless and serving every family in a practical way. Taking Wuzhou, Zhongfa, Xin Asia and other pharmaceutical factories as examples, a small booklet of essential medicines for a family should be set for housewives as a consultant. Then, taking Sanyou Hongxin and other cloth factories as examples, how to cut children's clothing, give away clothing and limit prices and how to allocate, the visiting staff should design it for housewives in the long run. In addition, for daily necessities, based on the most economical and effective small family calculations, how many kinds of goods should be prepared can also be considered for a single list for housewives' reference. All of these cannot be done without first going to the factory to see the details. Mr. Hu Xitu, Xu Xiaochu, Xiang Shengwu and Lu Zhixue all have rich experience in this matter. They believe that before the visiting staff set off, they should first listen to the talks of the leaders of the domestic goods industry and see the situation of each factory with their own eyes, and then they will have confidence in their chest and handle things easily. This is a real insight from experience. I sincerely hope that all visiting staff will practice what they preach and do it practically. I also hope that housewives will consult and discuss at any time when they encounter problems. If there is any dissatisfaction, speak directly so as to promote the improvement of the industrial sector. I respectfully contribute my words as an aid to the beginning of the home visit business.

Chun Qiu

Tidbits

— (Drunken Woodcutter)

A person with physical disabilities is the most painful and pitiful person in the world! If we are healthy, we should have sympathy for them; when necessary, we should also try our best to help them, so that their painful hearts can be deeply comforted; but in fact, this is not always the case.

We see actors in dramas pretending to be hunchbacks, cripples, blind people, etc., deliberately making them lifelike, winning laughter from the audience. I feel that society is always deformed! There are also some people who, when they see a beggar with a missing hand or foot begging for pity, quickly avoid them, not wanting to bring this hateful form into their eyes, leaving an unpleasant impression. This kind of person will never know how unfortunate the disabled are, and at the same time, they do not understand that human beings should have a responsibility to help each other!

"A plate of loose sand"! This humiliating hat has finally fallen on the heads of us Chinese people. Are we going to throw away this hat? What's more, in the current China with physical disabilities, how much we need a healthy group to help him! So that he can safely pass through the difficult times of wind and rain; then the great success of "mutual assistance" will shine a dazzling torch in the world!

The Ominous Character "West"

— Qing Qu

Speaking of this character "West", it originally did not have much meaning: if you want to study the origin of the character, then: it is nothing more than saying that its usage is obtained from pictograms; because the first character was just a bird perched on its nest, its head was still facing west, so its graphic was structured into the appearance of halogen, and later the seal script became regular script, and it became the "West" style. Who should study the original initial intention?

Now, the character "West", I say that there is some ominous bad luck coming to his direction. Don't you remember that when the communists were causing chaos in the past, didn't it happen in the two provinces of Jiangxi and Shanxi, causing misery to the people? It was because of the character "West" that they suffered from war and hardship. This is not long ago, and I think everyone can still remember it! If you talk about it farther away: from history, hum! Western Xia, Western Liang, etc., which one did not have to fight against the Han soil? Speaking of foreign countries, last year's Abyssinia was completely defeated by the violent Italy. Even if King A was unwilling to surrender and resisted for more than seven months, in the end, he just had to leave the motherland created and passed down by his ancestors and escape to other countries to save his life. Otherwise, the mustache on his mouth would inevitably be made into a board brush, and the black-clothed prime minister would have to brush his leather shoes. You think! Isn't that also suffering from the result of this "West" character!

Well, the recent military changes have happened in the southwest. In fact, it is only in Guangxi Province. Although there is no problem in Guangxi now; but isn't Spain also rebelling from the "Western" Morocco? You must know that this is no small matter. If you pull this hair, the whole body will really move. I am afraid that the prophecy of 1936 will unfortunately come true. What's the reason? Because this fuse is hard to guarantee that it is not the opening of the Second World War in Europe, and especially in Europe, a bloody drama will be staged in the future! If you don't believe it, please watch!

Patterns

— Zhu Ying

Since mankind has possessed the modern art of appreciation, everything is distinguished by lines. Lines are divided into straight lines, curved lines, thick lines, and narrow lines, and thus patterns arise. Although patterns are made up of uniform and coarse lines, in reality, things will not always fit the pattern. However, intelligent people have the ability to transform reality into patterns, or patternize them. Even the outline of a person can be transformed to have the lines of a pattern.

Women's new fashion publications are full of full-page new fashion patterns. Although some people suspect that patterns are just patterns, clever fashion designers can cut patternized new clothes according to the patterns. Girls wrap their non-patternized bodies in patternized new clothes, becoming a patternized and modern beauty. Three-dimensional shoulders, streamlined waist, turn fat and bloated into slender, and thin and skinny into plump. Appropriately arranging the lines, it is not difficult to turn ugliness into pattern beauty.

The skills of fashion designers are so superb. At the same time, beauticians can transform the faces of girls to fit the pattern beauty. Although everything on a person's face is born with it, small eyes can be transformed into not too big or too small, just right, and fit the lines and structure that should be in the face shape. The lines of the ears, nose, mouth, and lips can also be transformed according to the beautiful pattern. In the pattern, sometimes, in addition to the simple lines, for the sake of balance, several dots are needed for embellishment, so artificial moles or artificial freckles have to be used. And the eyebrows, which are generally considered the most difficult to solve by girls, have now invented glued-back artificial eyebrows. There is also eyelash glue for gluing eyelashes together. It is definitely not difficult to glue three or four eyelashes into one. Therefore, in ancient times, there were only true-to-life beauty paintings. This year, it has progressed to transforming into patterned beauties. This is the so-called not being dominated by the era, but mankind dominates the dynasty.

In ancient times, mankind was dominated by the era, so everything was left to natural progress. Three hundred years, four hundred years, still did not jump out of an original model, which was quite sparse and plain. This year, mankind is dominating the era. Even in terms of architecture, 1934 and 1935 each had their own patterns, and 1936 naturally has the pattern of 1936. Therefore, although the pattern is just a simple picture composed of several lines, in reality, patterns can be said to be one of the driving forces of modern civilization.

Eliminating Preconceptions About Famous Actors

— Si Su

What is performed on the stage is Peking opera, and what is performed by the Peking opera troupe in the amusement park is also Peking opera; however, the audience has a preconceived notion that the plays performed by the two sides cannot be regarded as equal, and the Peking opera in the amusement park is certainly not as good as the Peking opera on the stage.

This preconceived notion is not necessarily wrong. The amusement park is a place where all kinds of plays are mixed together. Although Peking opera occupies a major position, it is ultimately one part of the plays and cannot be compared with the stage. Moreover, actors with status are mostly unwilling to join the Peking opera troupe in the amusement park, fearing that this will damage their status. They would rather be the third or fourth rank on the stage than be the champion of the Peking opera troupe in the amusement park. This is another inconceivable preconceived notion held by the actors themselves.

However, to say that it is "naturally not as good" is not right. That is a preconceived notion, and it is not impossible to eliminate it forever. Like the current Xian Shi Amusement Park Peking Opera Troupe, the important actors they hire are all characters from the stage in the past: Wang Qichang is the son of the old actor Wang Hong, who specializes in performing Golden Leopard, Anti-Five Passes, Burning Cotton Mountain, Zhou Yu Returns to Heaven, and red student plays; Hu Yulou is the proud disciple of the old actor Tan Yueming, specializing in leaning on the handle, and is good at performing Pick Hua Che, Eight Great Hammers and other plays; Xia Junting is the grandson of Xia Yueshan and the nephew of Xia Yinpei, and is a famous and strong short-hitting martial artist; Zhao Kuiguan is a northern-style second flower, which is rare in the south. They are all famous actors, but now they are all hired by Xian Shi Amusement Park; on the one hand, Xian Shi Amusement Park is showing its brilliance, and on the other hand, famous actors can eliminate inconceivable preconceived notions, and jointly eliminate the preconceived notions of the public that the Peking opera troupe in the amusement park is naturally not as good as the stage, which is very admirable!

World Rare News

Japan's Tariff Barriers

— Ji Yun

Western-made cameras, lenses, films, and other photographic equipment require a tax of one hundred yuan for every one hundred yuan of original price. For example, a two-hundred yuan camera purchased in Japan requires a tax of fifty to seventy yuan. Travelers to Japan can only bring an old camera. When picking up friends at the ship, you must bring the camera to the customs inspection office for registration, otherwise there is a risk of being identified as smuggling and confiscated when you return and pass through the inspection office. According to customs officials, "The tariff on cameras is too high, and there is often smuggling, and old goods are easily missed." However, most of this smuggling is for greed, and it is possible to bring one or two more, but large-scale organized smuggling like ours is unprecedented in the world.

There are more than one hundred kinds of goods that are taxed according to the original price. The most important ones are Chinese wine, beer, fur, straw hats, gold glasses, clocks, gramophones, umbrellas, toys, etc. In recent years, these goods have almost disappeared. Chinese wine is divided into five-flavor skin, sorghum, and Shaoxing, and some Japanese shops repackage and sell them in Tianjin, decorating them like beer bottles. Taiwan is experimenting with manufacturing Shaoxing wine, which tastes light and astringent. A Shaoxing wine jar full of colored flowers, sold by a used goods store to a Japanese hotel for decoration, still costs four or five yuan. If it is full of wine, the price is considerable.

After the implementation of the "Specific Duty" in Showa 7, some are calculated by weight, and some are calculated by quantity. As a result, some taxes have increased by 35%. For example, a motorcycle originally had a tax of 93.6 yuan, but now it has become 126.36 yuan. There are about 800 kinds of goods with this kind of production rate, so the price of imported goods has to be expensive. Buying a Chinese-made thermos in Shanghai only costs half a yuan; going to Japan to buy a middle glass bottle costs one yuan. It is common for Japanese goods shipped to China to be cheaper than buying them in Japan.

Since Japan implemented the "gold export re-prohibition"; the exchange rate of Japanese gold has collapsed to one-third, and one American gold dollar is equivalent to about two Japanese gold dollars. Now one hundred Japanese gold dollars are only worth twenty American dollars. Therefore, after adding tariffs, even if European and American goods can be imported into Japan according to regulations, no one will buy them. Our country's tariffs cannot be completely autonomous due to certain relationships, so the tax is lower than in other countries. Moreover, after the price of silver has risen, it is very beneficial for the import of foreign goods, which directly hinders the fate of domestic goods; and some people still criticize our country's tariffs for being too high, which is really a pity.

Personal Vignettes

George Bernard Shaw's Eightieth Birthday

— Ying Dai

George Bernard Shaw, the contemporary British playwright known as the master of humor, turned eighty this year. July 26th is his birthday. But this time his eightieth birthday will not receive any gifts, and on the eve of his birthday, he refused to see guests and went alone to the墨尔飞 theater to visit his play Saint Joan being staged.

Old Shaw was born on July 26, 1856 in Dublin, England. The plays he wrote are often crowned with a long preface written by himself. In 1867, he went to London to work as a clerk in a telephone company. In 1884, he joined the Fabian Society of Socialism and contributed to various magazines. In 1895, he published drama reviews in the Saturday Magazine. He had long been advocating Ibsenism. He wrote many plays throughout his life, and most of his plays have been performed on stages in European countries with considerable success. He can indeed be called a warrior in the contemporary British literary world. In addition to writing plays, he has also published many works on political economy.

If we are not forgetful, then we will remember that in the spring of 1933, he traveled around the world and once came to Shanghai. At that time, the cultural circles in Shanghai expressed considerable welcome. However, Mr. Shaw stayed in Shanghai for only three or four days before heading north and transferring to Japan. In Japan, he made humorous remarks, indicating that it was a terrifying country, and gave the Japanese an impolite lesson.

Although he is a playwright, he does not like to invest in theaters. Until now, he still adheres to the belief that "a playwright should not invest in theaters." The reason for this is that recently a friend of his who runs an open-air theater wrote to him, asking him to invest in a partnership. In his reply, he not only refused to invest, but also greatly satirized his friend in a humorous tone.

His self-cultivation is peculiar, his thinking is superhuman, so he expresses dissatisfaction with everything in the current society. Although he is a believer in socialism, he often criticizes the actions of the communist parties of various countries. He once denounced Mussolini as a dilapidated car, who only knows how to talk big but cannot do big things. He also does not agree with his plays being put on the screen by Hollywood film companies, because he is afraid that the company will not use his dialogue at all after adapting the film script.

Now that Old Shaw is eighty years old, his spirit is still as vigorous as ever. He is okay when he doesn't talk to people, but when he talks to people, he speaks in a humorous tone, funny and ridiculous, making you laugh like crazy, and there is a knife hidden in the laughter. His words are also sarcastic everywhere, which will really make people laugh and cry!

Swapped Phoenixes

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 6: Iron Face Sees Kind Heart, Words Deceive Parrot, Emei Preserves Chivalry, Asks About Kunlun

Menglan listened to these words, nodded, and went back to her room. After that afternoon, Menglan herself didn't know what kind of illness she had gotten, only feeling restless. She reluctantly picked up a book to read, but she couldn't make out what the words were. To save trouble, she only pretended to be sick, so she could stay upstairs, not caring whether her family showed any attitude towards her. She stayed like this for two days, so that apart from her father, men and women all came upstairs to ask about her illness. But after seeing her, apart from seeing her deep frown, only the fact that she didn't apply face powder and her face was slightly yellowed could be considered a sign of illness. Everyone also understood that she was suffering from a mental illness. However, everyone only guessed half of the reason, thinking that it was caused by those wedding dresses. The only one who could guess a little more was her female classmate, Ms. Li Youmei. On the afternoon of the third day, Li Youmei came again. As soon as she entered the door, she saw Menglan supporting the table with her hands, holding her head. She was wearing a very thin, old blue wrinkled jacket, which made her look even more weak. She stood at the doorway and said with a smile: Is Lin Daiyu's illness getting better? Baoyu is here. Menglan turned her head and saw her, and smiled: You haven't even entered the door yet, and you're already joking with me. Youmei came in and held both of her hands at the same time, looking at her face. She frowned slightly and said: The sickness on your face is still very strong. Menglan smiled: Before you saw me, did you think I was faking my illness? Youmei smiled: How come our Miss Jiang opens her mouth with barbed words? As she spoke, she lightly patted her shoulder and said: But I don't blame you. You are full of unhappiness, and your complaints are easily triggered. Menglan sat down, leaning on a corner of the table with her, and asked with a bitter smile: How do you know I'm sick? I guess it's because I haven't been to school for three days, so you came to ask about me? Youmei smiled: No, I also have a little private matter to ask you about. Menglan smiled: You know more things than I do, yet you're coming to ask me about them. What is it? As she said this, Xiaoju came with a teapot to pour tea. Youmei didn't answer her words, but took a piece of paper from the table and wrote five words on it with a pen, Kunlun Ma Mole. Then she drew circles densely around the five characters with the pen, looked up at her face and smiled, asking: I don't understand this allusion very well, can you tell me about it? Menglan saw that Xiaoju had poured two cups of tea on the table and was already standing aside, looking at people with a smile, so she said: Little ghost! Go downstairs, what news are you planning to listen to here? Xiaoju said: I have an essay that I plan to use such an allusion, but I'm afraid I'm not using it properly. (75)

Special Telegraphic Edition

Several Points Worth Noting for Senders and Receivers After the Implementation of the New Rules

— Bao Zhen

The newly revised charging rules for place names and recipient addresses in Chinese telegrams (hereinafter referred to as "New Rules") are a new initiative in telecommunications this year, closely related to the public. The points worth noting for senders and receivers are described as follows:

1. Recipient's Name and Address Should Not Be Too Brief　Since the implementation of the New Rules on September 1st, many senders, due to the provision in the New Rules that the number of characters in the recipient's address in various Chinese telegrams, together with the number of characters in the place name, is counted as one character for every two characters, often try to reduce the number of characters in the recipient's address, or only write the recipient's name and omit the address, in order to save telegram fees. According to Article 35 of the current General Regulations for Domestic Telegram Operations, the sender must clearly state the recipient's address and name in detail. If the sender writes the recipient's address too briefly or only writes the recipient's name without an address, it not only violates the above regulations but also inevitably leads to delays. Because Chinese merchants commonly use characters such as "Tai," "Da," "Xing," "Sheng," "Chang," "Long," and "Kang" in their business names, and common people's names are often similar, common business names such as "Tai Chang," "Da Sheng," "Hua Xing," "Tai Kang," "Fu Long," and common names such as "Zhang Ying," "Wang Guodong," etc., often exist more than once in the same place. Telegrams with only the recipient's business name and no address, such as "Zhenjiang Da Sheng," and telegrams with incomplete recipient addresses, such as "Qingdao Feicheng Road Zhang Ying," may be delivered by the Zhenjiang or Qingdao Telegraph Bureau after efforts to find the recipient, but there may be several businesses with the same name "Da Sheng" in Zhenjiang, and there may be more than one resident named "Zhang Ying" on Feicheng Road in Qingdao, making it difficult to avoid misdelivery or misreceipt, or delaying the telegram delivery time due to repeated searches. Therefore, senders must not be greedy for the small benefit of saving a few telegram fees, which may delay the opportunity and defeat the original purpose of sending a telegram.

2. Charging Method for Chinese Place Names and Address Names　The General Regulations for Domestic Telegram Operations, printed by the Telecommunications Department of the Ministry of Communications in September 1935, charged separately for Chinese place names and address names (for example, the place name in ordinary Chinese telegrams, regardless of the number of characters, was charged as two characters, and the address name was charged as three characters if it did not exceed thirteen characters). The revised charging method for Chinese telegram address names counts the actual number of characters in the place name and recipient's address name together, charging one character for every two characters. For example, "Qiqihar East Street (253) Hua Zuguo" has a total of twelve characters, which should be charged as six characters. This charging method is simpler than the old rules.

3. Advantages of Registered Telegrams　The motivation and purpose of a recipient paying a fee to register at the telegraph office are to benefit themselves and others. The registration procedure is very simple. The recipient only needs to choose a character and pay the fee to the local telegraph office according to the regulations. All telegrams sent to the recipient from various places can use the registered character instead of the recipient's name and address. On the sender's side, it can not only save a few characters of telegram fees but also reduce the trouble of writing the recipient's address in detail, greatly increasing the speed of preparing and sending telegrams. On the recipient's side, since they have registered at the telegraph office, they can print the chosen registered character in advertisements or on letter paper as a commercial promotion. When sending the same telegram or sending a telegram to others, they can use the registered character instead of their full name, paying only for one character, which is more economical than using the full name. In addition, short registered telegrams take less time to transmit at the telegraph office, so senders and receivers using registered characters to send and receive telegrams greatly increase the speed of telegrams. After the implementation of the New Rules, some senders may think that for Chinese telegrams with short recipient addresses, the number of characters in the address name is only six or seven, which is charged as three or four characters for every two characters, which is not much more expensive than using a registered character, and they may no longer use registered characters. However, if registered characters are not used, the above-mentioned conveniences cannot be enjoyed, and when sending a telegram, it is necessary to consider how to write the recipient's address as briefly as possible in order to reduce the number of characters. However, telegrams with incomplete address names are prone to misdelivery, misreceipt, or delays, so senders should still use registered characters.

4. Standard for Telegram Rates Within the Province or to Other Provinces　Domestic telegram rates have now been changed to two types: within the province and to other provinces. Telegrams sent within the province are charged at the within-province rate, and telegrams sent to other provinces are charged at the to-other-provinces rate, which is very simple and clear. However, for telegrams forwarded by mail or delivered by special delivery, the telegram must be sent by the telegraph office closest to the recipient's location to the post office for forwarding, or delivered by a special delivery messenger hired by the telegraph office. Even if the recipient's location and the sending office belong to the same province, such as telegrams forwarded by mail or delivered by special delivery from Beiping to Nangong (Beiping and Nangong both belong to Hebei Province), the telegram must be transferred through the Dezhou Telegraph Bureau in Shandong during its transmission process. Therefore, it seems that there are some discrepancies in how the telegraph office should charge for this type of telegram. However, since the recipient's location "Nangong" and the sending location "Beiping" both belong to Hebei Province, the telegram should still be charged at the within-province rate. Conversely, if the recipient's location belongs to another province, even if the telegraph office in this province forwards the telegram by mail or delivers it by special delivery, the telegraph office must still charge at the to-other-provinces rate. The distinction between within-province and to-other-provinces rates should be based on the recipient's location.

Trial Implementation of New Long-Distance Telephone Services

Since the completion of the nine-province long-distance telephone project and the opening of communication locations in various provinces, China's long-distance telephone business has entered a stage of development. The more users there are, the simpler the procedures should be. Only then can the business develop, which is a logical trend.

According to the regulations, anyone who wants to send a long-distance telephone call, in addition to calling for communication, must report the other party's telephone number when registering. If the caller only knows the name and address of the person being called but does not know their telephone number, they cannot apply for registration and cannot communicate with them.

In addition, for pre-arranged calls, if the designated person being called is not available, resulting in failure to communicate, the caller must pay a fee to cancel the registration. If the caller must communicate, they will have to request a pre-arranged call again, which is uneconomical in terms of time and call charges.

In order to facilitate the public and promote business, the Ministry of Communications has made the following two improvements:

(1) If the caller only knows the name and address of the called user but does not know their telephone number, they can also apply for registration. If the reported user is found not to have a telephone installed, or the installed telephone has been renamed or transferred, or the name does not match the name listed in the telephone directory and cannot be verified, resulting in failure to connect, cancellation will be allowed free of charge.

(2) Regarding pre-arranged calls, when the caller registers, they may also request: "If the designated person being called is not available, resulting in failure to communicate, the telegraph office should notify the called user to inform the person being called: The caller hopes to receive a return call at a certain time." After the calling office accepts this request, it should notify the called office to do so. When the called office calls, if the designated person being called is not available, it should immediately notify the called user of the caller's location, name, address, or telephone number, and ask them to inform the person being called to follow the caller's instructions and return a call on time. At the same time, notify the calling office and ask the caller to pay the cancellation fee according to the regulations, without having to pay the call charge. It is said that the above two measures are scheduled to be implemented on a trial basis on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hankou direct circuits starting from October 1st.

Recent Improvements in Telegram Operations

— Zhen

1. Instructing All Bureaus to Carefully Handle Telegram Code Errors

The Telecommunications Department of the Ministry of Communications recently noted that some publications in the market that publish telegram codes and telegram rules have errors due to careless editing and proofreading, which can lead to mistakes if users are not aware of them. It has specifically instructed all bureaus that, in the future, when translating telegram codes, they should uniformly use the newly compiled Mingmi Telegram Code printed by the Ministry of Communications and must not use other types of codebooks in order to ensure accuracy and facilitate business.

2. Messengers Should Make Every Effort to Find and Deliver Telegrams

It has been found that there are often errors or changes of address in the names and addresses of recipients. When messengers deliver telegrams, they are often unable to make every effort to find and deliver them due to time constraints, resulting in telegrams not being delivered. In order to improve the situation, the Telecommunications Department has instructed all bureaus that, in the future, when messengers deliver telegrams, if there are errors in the recipient's name and address, they should make every effort to find and deliver them and should not make any excuses. However, when returning to the bureau, they can report the search and delivery situation to the dispatching officer. After verification, the time limit for the delivery can be cancelled, and detailed notes should be made in the delivery inspection form for future reference.

3. Handling Undeliverable Telegrams

It has been found that there is no fixed procedure for handling undeliverable telegrams, which is inconvenient in many ways. A method for handling undeliverable telegrams has now been established. When bureaus encounter undeliverable telegrams, in addition to notifying the sending bureau of the reason for non-delivery via public telegram for transmission to the sender and registering for future reference, they should also handle them simultaneously according to the following items: (1) Check the address and ask the postman of the postal office in the same area with original recipient name and address for details; (2) If the recipient's address is too brief to be verified by postal office, contact the highest postal office and ask for help; (3) Post announcement about telegram pick-up. In addition to the above, they should also kindly ask the local Chinese and foreign newspapers to publish the telegram pick-up news for free.

4. Specifying the Route for Telegrams Sent to Canada via International Wireless Telegraph

Regarding the route for telegrams sent to various locations in Canada via international wireless telegraph, the Telecommunications Department previously instructed in a telegram in July that, starting from that day, for telegrams sent to various locations in Canada via international wireless telegraph, if the sender specifies that they should be transmitted via the American Wireless Telegraph Company and the Canadian Pacific Telegraph Company circuits, Via Rca and CanadianPacific Telegraphs can be accepted. However, the route identifier Via Cgra-Rca and Cpr must be added for identification. If only the Traffic Company circuit is specified, the Via Cgra-Rca route identifier will still be used.

5. Promoting Ready-Made Social Telegrams　Ready-made social telegrams classify congratulatory or condolence messages into telegram texts printed on the back of the social telegram stationery. The sender only needs to specify which group of telegram text they want to send, and the sending bureau will transmit it according to the group number. The receiving bureau will then send the telegram text to the recipient, which is very convenient. However, the above-mentioned ready-made social telegram stationery cannot be opened for business until it has been sent. In addition to the bureaus under the jurisdiction of the Jiangsu and other telecommunications management bureaus that have already been opened, it is reported that the Ministry of Communications has sent the social telegram rules and ready-made social telegram stationery of the Guangdong and Gansu management bureaus. All bureaus will uniformly send and receive ready-made telegram text social telegrams to the Guangdong and Gansu regions starting from August 1st.

Recent Developments in the Expansion of Long-Distance Telephone by the Ministry of Communications (Continued)

(2) Provincial Trunk Lines

Among the aforementioned trunk lines and their connecting lines, some have been fully connected and interconnected, while others have only a section of the line connected and interconnected, with the remaining sections not yet connected. The detailed situation is not listed in detail. (Editor's note: The advertisement for the connection and communication of the long-distance telephone trunk line of the Minister of Communications published on the second page of this newspaper today can be consulted by readers) (End)

Reading Club

The Educational Value of Andersen's Fairy Tales

— Zheng

More than ten years ago, in the garden of Chinese children's literature in the news, several gardeners transplanted a fragrant and brilliant flower from Denmark. After some artistic cultivation, it bloomed in less than three to five years, attracting all the innocent and lively tourists, making them happy and amazed. ——This was the happiest period after Andersen's fairy tales were introduced into our country.

In recent years, this wonderful flower seems to have encountered the desolation of autumn, and it has gradually withered away. People see it and start shaking their heads. Some even say that it only has the beauty and fragrance of "art" but no practical educational benefits; some even say that its color and fragrance will poison young tourists.

Why did it encounter such misfortune?

The reason is that since it was introduced into China, most critics have only complimented it on the surface. They talk about how skillful the author's artistic skills are, how clever the writing method is, how innocent the thinking is, how lively the words are, etc. From the beginning, very few people have paid attention to the deep meaning and rich educational value contained in each work. Some even say that in order to achieve success in writing art, he deliberately abandoned all materials containing educational value. This is really a thankless and biased praise. In order to excessively highlight half of its value, they have erased the other half of its more important value. ——That is a major reason why people soon become tired of it.

In fact, as long as we carefully savor it and do not pay too much attention to its words and grammar, we can easily see the profound meaning contained in each of his fairy tales:

First, the inspiration of "love." This is almost an element present in every one of his works. It is not found in other fairy tales. He often has sentences of this kind: "The rain clouds just washed the ramie's face, and the sun shone on it, just like a child who had washed his face and was kissed by his mother." In his "A Mother's Story," he wrote that after a child was taken away by death, the mother went out to look for him and met a thicket of thorns. She asked him for directions. The thicket of thorns wanted her to press her chest tightly against the thicket to warm him, and then he would tell her. The mother pressed her chest tightly against the thicket of thorns to warm it; the thorns pierced her flesh, causing large drops of blood to flow out. But the thorns were warmed, drew out green leaves, and bloomed again in the dark winter night. "A mother's heart is so warm!" Later, in order to ask the lake for directions, she was willing to cry out two bright eyeballs for him. She was willing to cut off a head of black hair to ask an old woman for directions. She cried to death for her child, saying, "Give me back my child!" She hated it so much that she wanted to pull out all the flowers in the big greenhouse, but,

Death said, "Don't move them. You say you are so unhappy, but if you pull them out, it will make other mothers just as unhappy."

"Other mothers?" the poor mother said, and put down her hand.

For her own child, she was willing to sacrifice everything; but for all mothers, she had to forgive the sinful death. What a profound and great concept of "love" is implied to the children here! No matter how hard-hearted a child is, after reading this story, they will definitely draw tears of sympathy from the depths of their hearts! He also inspired his young readers: All love should be equal, regardless of wealth or poverty, without high or low. He said, "The starlight shines on all houses, on the rich and on the poor, with the same brightness and the same happiness." He said, "The sunlight kisses the blooming apple branches, and also kisses the yellow dandelions in the fields. They are all brothers, the sunlight kisses them——the poor flowers are the same as the magnificent flowers." When young readers read this kind of passage, how will their hearts be moved? What a good effect will this kind of emotion have?

Second, the inspiration of "wisdom." In his "That's for Sure," he wrote that a hen accidentally pecked off a feather, which was seen by others. After several rumors, it turned into "five hens plucked off all their feathers and died for love of a rooster." Isn't this clearly telling the children that many hearsay things in society are unreliable? Of course, we know that even the news recorded in many newspapers is unreliable, but children don't know this much, so isn't it a good idea to inspire them with an interesting story? He also wrote in "The Leapfrog": Flea, Cuckoo, and Leapfrog compete to see who can jump the highest. Flea and Cuckoo can only jump, and as a result, one jumped out of sight, and one jumped onto the king's face. They were all eliminated. Leapfrog is a thinker. He jumped diagonally onto the princess's skirt; at that time, the princess was sitting on a stool. So,

The king said, "There is nothing higher than my daughter, but he jumped on top of her, so he is the highest. Only those who have thoughts can think of it. Leapfrog makes us know that he has thoughts, he has brains, and he should get the princess."

On the surface, this story seems to be very funny and naive. But after reading this story, any child, in addition to letting out a burst of happy laughter, will definitely explore the reason why Leapfrog was able to get the princess in a serious attitude. Therefore, the two sentences "Because he has thoughts and has brains" are deeply imprinted in their minds. In other words, this story has implied to them: Any noble and hard-won thing can be achieved as long as you are willing to use your mind and brain. Isn't this a very solemn lesson?

Andersen is indeed most painstaking in expressing and storing this kind of implied meaning. Sometimes he selects humorous story materials and deliberately hides the educational components in an appropriate way to make the story more interesting and allow the readers to absorb the lessons invisibly. "The Emperor's New Clothes" is a good example. (This was originally adapted from Don Maonel's "Cunt Luoanor." Gu Junzheng's "Andersen Biography" and Zhao Jingshen's "Collection of Fairy Tale Essays" both mention the ingenuity of the author's adaptation.) He hides the lessons in the original story that are too obvious and difficult for children to absorb in more humorous and interesting words; but he deepens the satire. He not only says that the emperor is stupid, corrupt, and incompetent, but also implies that the so-called "vanity" is self-deception. This is also something that children can understand invisibly.

Third, the inspiration of "goodness." In Andersen's fairy tales, there are several that often have the style of Esho and Tolstoy's fairy tales, but also contain the fun of Grimm's fairy tales. This has an unexpected effect on the enlightenment of children's morality. He often uses scolding the wicked to induce children's "goodness." In "The Bad King," he wrote about a king who did all kinds of evil, often leading his rude soldiers to attack and loot everywhere, and everyone was afraid of him. Sometimes, after attacking a country, he would take all its wealth and tie the king of that country back to his palace, ordering him to kneel at the feet of himself or his ministers and serve them food. Later, he became so arrogant that he wanted to conquer God. But the first time, he was burned half to death by the fire of the angels; the second time, he built countless spaceships in seven years, preparing for a major attack. Just as he was about to get on the ship, many mosquitoes suddenly flew over and stung the king one after another; the king was furious, and the sword beside him also lost its effectiveness, so he ordered people to take a precious mosquito net and wrap his body in it, but a mosquito still drilled in, flew into the king's ear, and stung randomly; so the king's brain was poisoned, tearing open the mosquito net, tearing his clothes, and dancing naked in front of the soldiers, causing the soldiers to laugh. In the end, he said, "The king wanted to defeat God, but he was defeated by a mosquito like this." Here, he not only tried his best to reprimand a cruel and immoral tyrant, but also wanted to induce the young readers to laugh at the tyrant along with the soldiers, making them unconsciously say, "Who told him to be so bad"! At the same time, they received a lesson in their hearts that they "cannot be too bad." In the previous paragraph, writing about his abuse of the defeated king can further arouse their sympathy for the weak and make them aware of the pain of national subjugation.

In his fairy tales, there are particularly many places about satirizing the arrogant, perhaps because he wanted to vent his past frustrations of running into walls everywhere. But isn't the educational value contained in it the same?

In addition, there are several of his fairy tales that contain the idea of the masses, such as "The Little Match Girl," "The Candle," "The Angel," and "There Is Class," all of which are worth introducing to children.

In short, his fairy tales are by no means just a form of leisure that is read and forgotten. When his first fairy tale was published, he had already suffered thirty years of hardship in the world and had experienced the vicissitudes of life. There are sad stories and sweet dreams. Therefore, he had to comfort his remaining life by traveling. He intertwined the worldly wisdom and lessons he had learned over the years in his beautiful fairy tales. They not only grasp the hearts of the young, but also want to transform them before they suffer the hardships of the world: making boys stronger and girls more gentle. Who says Andersen's fairy tales have no educational value?

Everywhere the Sound of Insects Chirping: It's the Season for Studying Insects

— Gao Wenlan

Once autumn arrives, the corners of walls, in the grass, on bamboo fences, everywhere is filled with the sound of "Qu-qu-qu, ji-ji-ji." This sound is the orchestra of autumn insects; each plays its own beautiful music, making an otherwise calm autumn night, which easily evokes melancholy, quite lively. Therefore, whether great poets or ordinary people, everyone has a fondness for autumn insects.

Autumn insects are truly a type of insect worth studying. Even if you don't want to become an entomologist and don't want to put your heart into research, you'll probably still want to catch a few to keep on your desk to break the loneliness and for appreciation! So, let me introduce you to reading "Tales of Singing Insects," because this book is of great help to you whether you are studying or appreciating autumn insects.

This book is divided into three chapters. The first chapter is a general discussion of the sounds and meanings of singing insects. The second chapter is about summer cicadas, and the third chapter is about autumn night insects. First, it uses scientific research to introduce the morphology, life, and habits of a type of singing insect. Then, from the literary interest and musical realism, it makes an appreciative examination of the singing insects, with many musical scores of the singing insects' calls attached. Readers can study the pitch and tempo of their songs according to the score. Finally, it explains the methods of catching and raising autumn insects. If we follow these methods to catch a few to keep on our desk, accompanying us in a quiet study at night, there will certainly be a special kind of interest.

It seems that autumn is the world of insects. Not only is it filled with insect orchestras everywhere, but there are also especially many insects that are not musicians. When you are reading or writing at night under a lamp, many insects, big and small, black and green, fly to the light, as if accompanying your loneliness or disturbing your work. Of course, you find these insects annoying and wish you could use some method to kill them one by one. However, these insects are pitiful. They feel the pain of darkness, so they desperately fly to the light, dancing and rejoicing. Their lives end in this one night. Even the long-lived ones only last for a day or two. Because they are pitiful and short-lived, we don't have much interest in studying them. We can study other types of insects with longer lifespans besides singing insects. So, let me introduce you to reading "The Life of Insects" and "Insect Talks." The insects described in these two books are sometimes highly social, sometimes beneficial to humans, sometimes more cruel than wild beasts, sometimes surpassing the achievements of high jumpers and long jumpers in the World Olympics, and sometimes harmful to humans. In all their forms and colors, reading them is like walking into an insect exhibition, meeting Mr. Fabre, a white-bearded French entomologist, who sincerely guides us one by one. The book "The Life of Insects" uses an interesting tone, first using scientific research to explain everything about them, and then using literary interest to write about stories related to humans. The book "Insect Talks" details the types and living habits of each insect. It is a so-called scientific essay and also a special book for studying insects.

When studying a subject, the season is very important. Therefore, in general textbooks, plum blossoms are always discussed in spring, and lotus flowers are discussed in summer. There is never a case of discussing plum blossoms in summer and lotus flowers in spring. This is because of the seasonal relationship, which is convenient for people's research. Autumn is the season for studying insects, so reading these books now should feel particularly interesting. If you like to catch singing insects to raise, then you must keep these books on your desk and browse them frequently.

Knowledge Nourishment for Young People

— Wei Qiangling

Scientific essays, which were once popular for a while, now seem to have disappeared like fish after a heavy rain.

I very much hope that there will be such works in bookstores to satisfy my desire for knowledge. Sometimes, when I see something I don't understand, and the author writes it out vividly and clearly, how surprised I am!

Every Sunday afternoon, something like candy lures me to go to various bookstores to search for such works.

"Finally, I found them!" In the bookshelf of the Kaiming Bookstore, I found four books by the Soviet youth writer Ilyin. These books were like several lively and naughty children, all opening their arms and laughing there. I excitedly picked up a thicker one, "Man and Mountain," and opened it to read. I learned that it was about how to use human abilities to fight against nature, to manipulate natural forces with scientific laws, and to make natural forces obey human will. It described the struggle to transform deserts, create new plants, make living maps, harness rivers, and change the weather, explaining that natural forces are not scary things, but our dear resources, and it all depends on human use. He used a light and lively tone, like an older brother writing to his younger siblings, cordial and thoughtful. It's ridiculous, at that time I forgot that I was by the bookshelf in the bookstore, and I read two or three chapters in one breath. Finally, driven by the desire to possess, "I'd rather freeze!" I took part of the money my family sent me to buy autumn clothes and bought back these four beloved books. I spent a week's worth of evenings exploring and reading them all. It turned out that the other three books also very kindly told me many rich pieces of knowledge that I didn't know.

I feel that my behavior was not wrong, nor was I fooled by the bookstore; because I got some rich knowledge that I didn't have before.

The greatest success of these few books is that they can explain complex and mysterious things simply and clearly, and describe the truth of the world with simple and vivid writing.

Van Loon writes about the evolution of mankind from a historical standpoint, which easily gives people a sense of ordinariness; Fabre uses a dialogue format to write about natural science, which requires people to understand deeply; Ilyin, on the other hand, has another way of writing. He uses vivid stories to describe difficult-to-understand emerging sciences, which can capture the reader's full attention. This is where he is more advanced than the two. The books he wrote are the nourishment of knowledge for our young people. We need books written in this way, I can't help but think.

Editor's note: All four scientific stories by Ilyin have been re-translated into Chinese by Mr. Dong ChunCai and published by Kaiming Bookstore. The first type "One Hundred Thousand Whys" is priced at 35 cents; the other three types "Man and Mountain," "Black and White," and "What Time Is It?" are now sold at special prices, please check the advertisement.

Publication News

1. "New Youth" Volume 2, Issue 7, Appendix

"New Youth Reader" Preview

The "New Youth" bi-monthly published by Kaiming Bookstore has been extremely popular with general young readers since its publication. The editors of the magazine originally had a plan to print a "separate appendix" each year to be distributed to subscribers of the magazine. As the separate appendix for the first year of publication, it was originally intended to select some articles suitable for young readers from the works of many contemporary writers, named "New Youth Reader", for new youth to read. Unexpectedly, after starting the selection, it was felt that this work was not easy. Because for a reader specifically for young people, first, the selected articles must be aimed at young people; second, the selected articles must have direct benefits for young people. If these two levels cannot be achieved, the selection work becomes meaningless. So, the direction was changed, and writers were asked to select an article themselves according to the previous two standards; and add a "preface" to explain the motivation, main points, etc. of the article, so that readers can understand more closely. There are now articles by twenty contemporary writers, arranged in new size four fonts with about two hundred pages, and bound separately, scheduled to be published on Double Ten Day (October 10th) and sent to subscribers at the same time as Volume 2, Issue 7 of "New Youth." This reader is exclusively for subscribers of "New Youth" and is "not for sale". If you want to get it, please subscribe to the "New Youth" bi-monthly as soon as possible. The "New Youth" bi-monthly is originally the best regular publication for young people across the country.

2. "Zhiyan" Issue 25 Published

Special Issue in Memory of Mr. Taiyan

Mr. Zhang Taiyan lived in Wuxia and founded the Zhang Clan National Studies Lecture Society; at the same time, he published the "Zhiyan" bi-monthly, which was edited by the lecture society. The writers in it are all famous writers. Since its publication, scholars at home and abroad have all rushed to see it first. Recently, after Mr. Taiyan passed away, his disciples, adhering to his instructions, continued to run the lecture society and continued to publish "Zhiyan". The 25th issue will be specially published as the "Special Issue in Memory of Mr. Taiyan" on September 16th. The number of pages has increased to four times. The most valuable work in it is the final manuscript of Mr. Taiyan's "Supplements to the Ancient Text Book of Documents," and Mr. Taiyan's own description of the order of his academic studies. Starting from this special issue, Kaiming Bookstore will be the general agent for distribution in six places: Shanghai, Nanjing, Hankou, Changsha, Beiping, and Guangzhou. The special issue is priced at 60 cents, the annual subscription for 24 issues is three yuan, and the half-year subscription for twelve issues is one yuan and sixty cents. The special issue is not priced separately. The retail price of each issue is fifteen cents.

3. Regarding the "Zhang Clan's Works"

The Zhang Clan Series was previously circulated in the world as a woodcut edition from the Zhejiang Library. Mr. Wu Jianzhai of Beiping and others also published a sequel to the Zhang Clan Series to supplement the missing parts of the main edition. It includes "Master Sima Qian's Explanation of the Ancient Text Book of Documents," "Supplements to the Ancient Text Book of Documents," "Questions and Answers on the Doubts of the Spring and Autumn Annals: Zuo's Commentary," "Da Han Chang Yan," etc. The "Examination of the Newly Discovered Three-Body Stone Classics" in one volume is handwritten and photocopied by Zhang's disciple Qian Xuantong, which is very precious. Now, Zhang's disciples have also compiled the third series of Zhang's Works, which will merge the main edition and the sequel and be published by Shanghai Kaiming Bookstore and submitted to the Ministry of Interior for registration according to law. It is heard that the main and sequel editions will be reduced to zinc plates from the original printed editions, and the gentlemen of the Zhang Clan National Studies Lecture Society in Suzhou will add punctuation to the main edition (according to the sequel edition has been punctuated); the third series will be meticulously arranged and proofread by Kaiming Bookstore. Once the entire book is plated and proofread, it will be sold at a special price.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking

Hitler's Famous Words

— Fang

At the eighth annual meeting of the German Social Party on the tenth, Hitler took the stage to deliver an important speech, first saying that all great struggles in the world, in short, are nothing more than mankind's instinct for conservation and the trend of national survival. Down to the modern era, all struggles, tracing their origins, are also determined by the survival purposes of some nations. Hitler's speech was really concise. I not only agree with it one hundred and twenty percent, but also agree with it two hundred and forty percent.

The world today is completely a world of power. How much power and influence you have determines how much territory you can protect. If you have no power or influence, even the land you should protect cannot be protected. Assuming you have sufficient power and great influence, you can take the territory of others as your own. The so-called world of the survival of the fittest is the world today.

But there are two kinds of survival, one is the survival of the strong, and the other is the survival of the weak. The survival of the strong is not satisfied with the existing territory, so they seek colonies or reclaim colonies to replenish their nourishing raw materials and support their people. But the weak should also seek survival and protect their existing territory and existing nourishing materials. Originally, there was something called justice and public law in the world. Now, there is no such thing as justice and public law. There is only survival, only power, and nothing else besides power.

Originally, there was something called the International Court of Justice, the Covenant of the League of Nations, naval treaties, disarmament conferences, and all the clauses of the alliance, which were still maintained on the surface. Now, they have been torn apart, torn up, and thrown into the Eastern Ocean. Everything, everything, only seeks power. Therefore, looking up at the countries of the world today, which country is not strengthening its military and expanding its armaments? The Japanese say that other countries are not allowed to interfere within one country, and the Americans say that their military equipment will be limited by heaven. This saying is not bad at all. In the world of power, only power can deal with it.

But if our country uses power, other countries also use power. Using power to deal with power, then power naturally has differences. The so-called strong will be restrained by the strong. Assuming that one originally does not advocate power, one will naturally be defeated by power. Assuming that one likes to advocate power, but one's ability is relatively small, one will be defeated by the stronger. But turning back to think, if strong countries want to survive, why don't weak countries want to survive? If strong countries want to protect, why don't weak countries want to protect? But what do weak countries use to protect themselves? Do you use justice to protect yourself? Justice has escaped beyond the world. Do you use humanity to protect yourself? Now is an inhumane world. Will you use the clauses of the alliance to protect yourself? The clauses of the alliance have long been waste paper. Then what do weak countries use to protect themselves? It is only hot blood, only black iron, only the unified spirit of the whole country, and a firm and unyielding attitude. It is truly said that if you want my heart, I want your internal organs, fight to the death, and fight until blood flows into rivers. In today's world, this is the only way to deal with it. There is no talk of friendship, no possibility of getting along well, mostly false masks and deception. Hitler's words are…

Short-Term Elementary School (Continued)

— Ma Jia

Tomorrow afternoon, I will walk from West Shanghai to Zhabei. With a joyful heart, I stepped into the school. The short-term elementary school does not charge tuition, and also gives books, pens, and ink to the children! The children who come to study are all poor, which is what I like, they are also receiving education!

There is still half an hour before class, and my heart is jumping in my chest. I am thinking that I want to turn them into the little heroes in my ideal, those poor children! I am about to see you.

When the bell rang, my heart jumped even more violently. I carried the roster and walked into the classroom. I saw a group of children in ragged clothes all sitting as straight as arhats. Their eyes were all looking at me—looking at me timidly. This made me a little sad. I shouted to them:

"Won't you smile?"

Some of them smiled, and some whispered: "This teacher is quite interesting!" I started calling names, and their names were all very common, like "A Mao," "A Gou," "Little Gou," "Little Mao," "Monk!"...

The classroom doorway was crowded with elementary school students who had just been dismissed. They heard the names that were only shouted at home, but now they were actually being shouted from the teacher's mouth in the classroom. This couldn't help but make them burst into laughter. I shook my head at them, but they ignored me and continued to laugh. I was a little angry.

In order to understand the family situation of those children, I patiently asked them one by one. They were all unadorned and didn't feel anything:

"My dad is a tailor's clerk!"

Those young masters outside the door laughed again, and said in a sarcastic tone: "Ah, a tailor's clerk!" I was very unhappy and glared at them.

The second one who answered me was: "My dad is a cobbler!"

Those young masters outside the door not only burst into laughter, but also shouted loudly: "Can you make me a pair of shoes?"

At this point, I stood up and wanted to drive those young masters away, but the so-called wild children in the classroom shouted: "You know you have money to study! What are you showing off!..."

I quickly closed the classroom door and said to them: "Don't quarrel! Let's read our books! I believe that although we only study for three hours, what we get is definitely more than them! Children! Just be attentive! Be attentive!..."

"We will be attentive!..."

In their shouting, I felt a burst of disappointment: Isn't it? Who separated them so far?

Is it that classroom door?… (The End)

Autumn Sketches

— Green Leaf

Autumn is a clear and lovesick season, which is different from spring and summer because of that characteristic. Although spring has the tenderness of the youth age of the season, it does not have the high and clear autumn sky, which makes people have a kind of deep and far-reaching melancholy. Although I am not a poet or writer, the praise for autumn is a melancholy season of entrusting affections. It is autumn that brings insight to the eyes.

Page 23

First, autumn is also a cloudy season. Looking at the clouds from time to time is indeed a unique pleasure: the clouds in autumn are like an oil painting in the style of medieval Spain, depicting the sky with a heroic and vigorous mood, adding a lot of color to the autumn itself. Standing on the small building, looking at the flowing and rolling white clouds on the treetops of the parasol trees, stopping and gazing at them rolling in the long sky, changing in an instant, this can also be regarded as one of the autumn scenes.

And the white clouds and grey dogs in the autumn sky are difficult to predict. Sometimes it is like a shepherd boy and a group of snow-white sheep wandering on the seaside at dusk, sometimes it is like a deserted island at sea and scattered sails, which makes people unable to grasp the magic of the magician's ever-changing tricks. If we sip tea in a small building and discuss the experience of watching clouds and the sayings of ancient and modern times, this is just a little bit, but it is also unique and elegant. This can be regarded as a small feeling of watching clouds.

Secondly, the autumn sunlight is bright. In the morning, walking on the seaside, the sea surface shining with autumn sunlight and the golden shells are smiling brightly and tenderly, which can warm your heart. And on the withered and yellow dead branches and on the red leaf tips, the autumn sunlight is even more cheerful and bright. Strolling on the quiet path paved with the bright autumn sunshine, everything makes you feel complacent and thoughtful, thinking about the autumn of childhood...

At least in my case, autumn is a season I like, making people remember and miss it.

Life

— Yi Bei

"Human Grass" One

Living in this remote and poor place, the biggest purpose, of course, is to make a not-so-small concession to this incompatible and difficult-to-deal-with life; and what is unexpected is that the form of life, even if it has been simplified to the point where it is almost primitive, yet the wind of the evil century from the outside has not reduced its difficulty by a single bit. And the customs here are so closed and disgusting that it is hard to believe its existence. Because, in this remote corner, the mountains and clouds, those people, those elusive prayers and dreams, are all covered with a thick layer of medieval ignorant dust: there. The distance between the destiny of nature and human wisdom is still so far away. People walk on endless muddy roads in a life of hardship and cruelty. The vast and boundless clouds and sky only give them a feeling of vastness and boundlessness. And the road of their lives, their cruel struggle, is also so vast, empty, broad, and boundless...

However, in this corner of the old and withered world, there are also smart people. They picked up some scraps of fraud and trickery from the vast, evil fighting world. So, when they retreated from the evil fighting and prosperous world, they quietly climbed into this corner of the "outside world", built churches, cheated to get manors, and brought opium, white flour and other things, brought strange gambling tools, and brought a philosophy of life that could add artificial ignorance to primitive ignorance...

And since I lived here, that teaching gentleman who wears the same suit jacket bought from "Hong Kong" all year round, and those tattered long pants without pockets, had to be said to be one of the "smart" people. The men call him "teacher" and call the other incredible people "master", etc. Because, habitually, in this corner, smart people often dominate those "little guys", and that one who is called a teacher, he knows how to quickly improve his life, not only make it "good" but also make it "rich", and he is indeed quite "rich".

When he first came, it is said that he brought a lot of shiny silver coins. He sent them to the people he had carefully selected. As he himself said, he would not do anything in vain. So, soon he separated some other money and deposited it in the opium dens, churches, and poor tenants... By the second year, he became the boss of the opium dens, an important person in the church, and the owner of the land.

No one can imagine him in the dead of night, alone in his windowless hut, checking the large and small silver coins "earned" in a day, a month, or a year, one by one, and secretly hiding them away: but that smile, those strange, perhaps a little terrible smiles, were often carved on his face—that sharp and dry face, on his forehead, at the corners of his mouth, carved with skin wrinkles that were so sharp they were almost like wooden statues, arched, so rigid and even, simply not like what a living being should have; so, at a time when my life was declining even more terribly, he said those terrible "smart" words to me in that expression: "Ah, don't worry at all; life is not a big deal, people can't easily starve to death. You see, have there ever been birds falling from the sky because they starved to death...?"

And really, that proud and relaxed voice made me feel no small surprise. It is rare for birds to fall from the sky because they starve to death; but on the ground, on this human ground, I have seen whole groups of people die of starvation, and that is not just once. I am often threatened by life, so, when finally, that teacher noticed the small gold commemorative ring that I had stubbornly guarded for five years on my hand, and proposed to exchange it with me for five silver coins in my "crisis," I couldn't help but laugh blankly. What is the value of past memories? And when life seems "easy" to a "smart" person, it feels very burdensome to a clumsy person. I like to see the ease of life, but I hate even more the "smartness" of that teacher who used the analogy of birds to "comfort" or ridicule me...

Autumn Rain

— Er He

Rain, rain, yes, it's raining softly outside the window at this moment…, friend: perhaps you live in the city, perhaps you live in the countryside, but this doesn't matter, in any case, you should also be experiencing the rain. In the countryside, perhaps you are in a small house built of mud, or perhaps in a simple house covered with straw? In the city, then perhaps you are in a narrow, cluttered garret, or perhaps in a spacious and magnificent skyscraper? Perhaps you are frowning, biting your fingers, lamenting the soft rain, but the soft rain does not stop because of your lament, it deliberately goes against you, just falling gently, falling…. Friend, how are you? Can you bear this heavy, oppressive melancholy? I know you will hate it, or perhaps you simply light a cigarette, watching the thick white smoke curl from your nostrils, but unfortunately, perhaps the smoke makes you sink into old dreams. Perhaps old wounds are discovered, perhaps many faded stories are dancing before your eyes, perhaps a strong sadness is brewing. Yes, I know, you will drink, because drinking can dispel sorrow. But in reality, you will prove yourself deceived. The flood of sorrow comes even more fiercely. Perhaps you will unintentionally hum ancient verses: "Wine enters the sorrowful intestines, each drop turns into tears of longing." But, it is equally unhelpful. Friend: How are you? You should look at the soft rain outside the window again…, but this time, I know you are not frowning or biting your fingers, because you have no anxiety, let alone any strength. You are just silent, you are overwhelmed by endless thoughts.

Then dusk comes. On banana leaves, on paulownia leaves, the sound of rain is like the sound of insects, rustling. How are you, friend: perhaps you inadvertently recite the verses you used to know by heart: "Three or two banana trees outside the curtain, what can one do late at night?"! "Paulownia trees and fine rain, dripping until dusk, how can this state be described with just one word of sorrow?" But what can you do, friend, perhaps you open the door and look outside, but the courtyard is dark and gloomy, only the rustling rain occasionally falls on your sleeves. What to do, friend: I know you are silent. Retreat to the bed, still quietly fall asleep, you close your eyes, expecting colorful dreams, but before long, you seem to feel that you must open your eyes. When your eyes open, you think, it's late at night, go back to sleep, so you turn your body to the side, banishing all thoughts from your mind, but your mind doesn't listen, it insists on thinking, so you wish you could smash your head, so you simply get up, walk to the table, wanting to write a few lovely verses or lyrics, perhaps you succeed, perhaps you don't. Then you think about trying to sleep again, but then many things come to mind again, perhaps thinking about someone you just parted with, perhaps thinking about many years ago,… thinking, thinking, friend: can you sleep again? You murmur, "Thin quilt, small pillow, cool weather, suddenly feel the taste of parting. Toss and turn, counting the cold watches, getting up and going back to sleep. After all, can't sleep, one night is as long as a year." You must think this is your own writing. Perhaps you drank too much, perhaps you are really too sentimental, you cry, sobbing, like a child with a grievance with nowhere to vent. You murmur, "Tonight the dim lamp shines obliquely, still, after the autumn rain clears, the tears don't clear." You simply don't want to sleep anymore. You wait for the fresh sunshine of tomorrow.

Dawn comes, but it is still softly raining…. You will weakly murmur, "Tears before the pillow, rain before the steps, dripping until dawn across the window." But you are too tired after all, you are like a dying cold butterfly without a shred of strength, you lie down, you finally stop. In your dream, you may still be sad. Friend: You have probably tasted enough of the autumn rain, right? At this moment, you are already snoring, along with the soft sound of rain outside the window.
