Storytelling

Cao Xiao's Yellow Dragonfly

China-West (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening Chapter "The Fate of Tears and Laughter - Flogging Fengxi"

The general's angry eyes are wide open, his hand wielding a rattan whip, walking upstairs. I don't care about you. Last night, I went to heaven on business. You actually secretly left the house. Ah, you lowly person. Crack a whip. Utter a curse. His hand waves, his eyes follow, not stopping. I saw her snow-white skin and cloud-like hair in disarray. Her clothes are disheveled, revealing her chest. Fengxi hears. Trembling. Her body is covered in fragrant sweat. There are ears on the other side of the wall, beware of being noticed. How could there be no eavesdroppers outside the window? Who knew that the angry general heard this and sneered two or three times. I understand everything in your heart. Could it be that you are continuing your old relationship with a secret lover? I think you, living in a humble alley, are lowly. Singing and playing clappers for a living. Now you haven't changed your usual ways. I'm just afraid that the fox's tail will still be revealed. I thought you had changed your ways and disguised yourself as a scholar. Becoming a respectable female student. Coming here, enjoying wealth and luxury. Wearing fine clothes and eating jade delicacies, happy. Who knows that you have a born seductive nature. Can't hide, the fleeting affair. You actually gave me a green hat in secret. Wormwood is not a noble plant. Only comparable to roadside willows and wall flowers, wild grass. How can a sparrow become a phoenix? Of course, you are not worthy of being a madam.

Na Ruiting's Three Smiles

Lin Ji (1220) 9:05 PM to 10:00 PM

Opening Chapter "The Pipa of Xunyang"

Sima Xiangshan went down to Jiangzhou. Anchoring at the ancient head of Xunyang Bo at night. Saying goodbye sadly together. Reed flowers and maple leaves in the late autumn Jiang. Thinking of myself, I am sadly exiled like duckweed. Seeing off the boat sailing on the water. Looking at the moon on the Jiang water, it is already the second watch, the watchtower sounding. Suddenly hearing the mournful sound of strings starting, asking where the sadness is like a complaint. Therefore, the host and guests approached a neighboring boat. Calling her to move her boat to meet with half shyness. Seeing that the old Qiuniang is still charming. Adding a cup of wine to the table. Only listening to her, narrating her life's glory and old dreams. But unfortunately, spring flowers and autumn eyes cannot stay. The bronze strings are pressed, the silver nails are adjusted. Who knows that the mandarin duck curtain is empty, longing for the jade hook. Past events are unbearable to look back on. Unspeakable, several times the whole story from the beginning. Seeing her, the remaining rouge and powder are in vain regret. The blood-stained pomegranate skirt. Later, the carriages and horses gradually became scarce, sad and cold. How could I marry a husband from Fuliang? Like the palace fan discarded by the autumn wind. The missing moon is difficult to invite the jade axe to repair. Know that since ancient times, the entertainment venue is the same as the officialdom. Cang Sang changes easily and leisurely. I am also the same lost visitor in the world. Knowing each other at the end of the road, tears in both eyes. However, the pipa on the river has thousands of years of hate. I persuade you to play another song. Just because I have nothing to give you, so I make a new song. Waiting for the song to end and the wine to run out, people leave. Hearing the sound of the horses returning. Feeling that, the red face and green shirt shed tears.

Zhou Zhenyu's Righteous Demon Biography

Yuan Chang (1120) Midnight 0:45 AM to 1:30 AM

Opening Chapter "Spring Boudoir Complaint Lyrics" (Mimi Collection Creation Issue)

Curved railing, curved wall. Winding through the corridor. Walking through the fragrant path. A burst of wind brings a burst of fragrance. Butterflies fluttering. Swallows in pairs. Branches and leaves casting shadows of willows. But seeing that the peach blossoms are bright like brocade. Willow catkins are fluttering and dancing. And hearing the sound of iron horses rattling, startling the larks and drums. The curtain hook is not seen rolling up heavily. The curl of incense is faint and fragrant. Thinking of Nu Nu, I am day and night haunted by old hatred. Tired and lazy to embroider mandarin ducks. Jade comb does not care for silky hair. Precious mirror is lazy to apply light makeup. All day long, sitting alone in the boudoir, the sound is quiet. Aroused, lying listlessly on the bed. Then call, add firewood to the stove. The maid is busy preparing medicine. But listening, the wind and rain are heavy outside, the lonely lamp is dim, the night is long. Can not help him, the heart is right and wrong to think. Whispering to oneself. I remember, my Qingqing had it before. Only hope to accompany Xiao Lang day and night. Unexpectedly, the wind and waves rose in the vast sea of love. I was harmed, a lonely shadow alone. I am inch by inch, the sun is broken inch by inch. Miss you, tears streaming down. From now on, the road is long, I can't wait for news. Tears are breaking my heart. I feel, bitter rain is miserable and lonely. The sorrowful wind is cold and sad. Only the lamp remains, throwing red beans. Quietly, the silk is faded. Poor me, I hate my life is thin. Tears wet the silk robe. Try to see, the green grass in front of the court is over the years. I only hate that the threads of love are not long. The dream is vague, familiar with the yellow millet.
